GB 18030 一 2022	GB 18030 to 2022	yes
信息扩术 ”中文编码字符集	Information Augmentation Chinese encoded character set	yes
1 本文件规定了信息技术用的中文图形字符及甚二进制编码的十六进制表示 。	1 This document specifies the hexadecimal representations of Chinese graphic characters and even binary encoding for information technology.	yes
本文件适用于中文和其他文字图形字符信息的处理、交换、存储、传给、显现 、输入和输出。	This document is suitable for the processing, exchange, storage, transmission, display, input and output of Chinese and other text and graphic character information.	no
本文件适用于为具备中文和其他文字图形字符信息化处理及交换功能的技术类产品,包括但不限于以输入法、光学字符识别 (OCR)、编辑 校对、机融翻诺、语音合成、文字转写、乔能写作等为代表的软件产品 , 以及以计算机、通信终端设备、电子书阅读毅、学习机等为代表的便件产品 。	This document is applicable to technical products with Chinese and other text and graphic character information processing and exchange functions, including but not limited to software products represented by input method, optical character recognition (OCR), editing and proofreading, machine translation, speech synthesis, text transcription, Qiao Neng writing, etc., as well as convenience products represented by computers, communication terminal equipment, e-book reading Yi, learning machines, etc.	no

下列本语和定义适用于本文件 。	The following terms and definitions apply to this document.	no
3.1 字符 character	3.1 character character	no
供组织、控制或表示数据用的元素集合中的一个元素。	An element in a collection of elements used to organize, control, or represent data.	no
3.2 编码字符 coded character	3.2 Coded character	no
字符 (3.1) 及其编码 示。	Characters (3.1) and their encoding.	no

3.4 字汇 repertoire	3.4 Word repertoire	no
用编码字符 (3.2) 集表示的一个指定的字符(3.1)集合 。	A specified set of characters (3.1) represented by a set of coded characters (3.2).	no

GB 18030 一 2022	GB 18030 to 2022	no
4 字汇	4 Word repertoire	no
4.1 概述	4.1 Overview	no
本文件收录的字符以单字节、双字或四字节编码 。	The characters included in this document are single-byte, double-word, or four-byte encoded.	no
单字节部分收录了 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的 0x00~0x7F 全部 128 个字符 。	The single-byte part contains all 128 characters of 0x00~0x7F of GB/T 11383 to 1989.	no
4.3 双字节部分	4.3 Dubyte Section	no
双字节部分收录了 GB/T 2312 一 1980 中的全部图形字符 GB/T 13000 中的CJK 统一汉字以及部分图形字符。	The double-byte part contains all the graphic characters in GB/T 2312-1980 and the CJK unified Chinese characters in GB/T 13000 and some graphic characters.	no
双字节部分的字符按照附录 A 的规定。	The double-byte portion of the character is as specified in Appendix A.	no
其中,表意文字描述符的图形、代码位置和功能应符合附录 B 的规定 。	Among them, the graphics, code location, and function of the ideogram descriptor should comply with the provisions of Annex B.	no
注: GB/T 13000 对中国、日本、恩国、越南等国家和地区使用的汉字统一编码。	Note: GB/T 13000 is a unified encoding of Chinese characters used in China, Japan, Enguo, Vietnam and other countries and regions.	no
具备独有抽象字形的汉字,赋予单独的代码位置;来源不同而抽象字形相同的汉字, 则赋予共用的代码位置。	Chinese characters with unique abstract glyphs, given a separate code position; Chinese characters with different origins and the same abstract glyph are given a common code location.	no
经过编码的汉字称为CJK 统一汉字 CCJK Unified Ideographs,其中 CJK 表示中国、日本、韩国。	The encoded Chinese character is called CJK Unified Ideographs, where CJK stands for China, Japan, Korea.	no
4.4 四字节部分	4.4 Four-byte portion	no
四字节部分收录了上述双字节字符之外的 GB/T 13000 中的 66 个CJK统一汉字(9FA6 一 9FEF，不包括 9FB4~9FBB 的8个字符)、CJK 统一汉字扩充 A、CJK 统一汉字扩充 BCJK 统一汉字扩充 C、 CJK 统一汉字扩充 DCJK 统一汉字扩充下 .CJK 统一汉字扩充 F 和已经 在 GB/ 工 13000 中编码的少数民族文字的字符。	The four-byte part contains 66 CJK unified Chinese characters in GB/T 13000 in addition to the above double-byte characters (9FA6 to 9FEF, excluding 8 characters of 9FB4~9FBB), CJK Unified Chinese Character Expansion A, CJK Unified Chinese Character Expansion BCJK Unified Chinese Character Expansion C, CJK Unified Chinese Character Expansion DCJK Unified Chinese Character Expansion Under . CJK Unicode Extensions F and characters from minority scripts already encoded in GB/Gong 13000.	no
四字节部分的字符按照附录 C 的规定 。	The four-byte portion of the character is specified in Appendix C.	no
5 总体结构	5 General structure	no
正文中凡数字前标有 0x 的表示采用十六进制,未标有 0x 的表示采用十进制。	In the text, where a number is preceded by 0x, hexadecimal is used, and non-marked 0x is decimal.	no
附录中凡编码的表示均采用十六进制,其他数字的表示均采用十进制。	All codes in the appendix are represented in hexadecimal, and other numbers are represented in decimal.	no
单字节部分采用 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的编码结构,使 用 0x00~0x7F 码位。	The single-byte part adopts the coding structure of GB/T 11383 to 1989, and uses 0x00~0x7F code points.	no
双字贡部分采用两个八位二进制位串表示一个字符,其首字节码位从 0x81 一 0xFE, 尾字节码位分别是 0x40 一 0x7E 和 0x80 一 0xFE。	The double-character tribute part uses two eight-bit binary bits to represent a character, with the first byte code points from 0x81 to 0xFE, and the last byte code points from 0x40 to 0x7E and 0x80 to 0xFE.	no
四字节部分采用 GB/工 11383 一 1989 未采用的 0x30 一 0x39 作为对双字节编码扩充的后缀,编码范围为 0x81308130 一 0xFE39FE39。	The four-byte portion uses GB/11383-1989 0x30-0x39, which is not used in 1989, as a suffix for double-byte encoding encoding, which ranges from 0x81308130 to 0xFE39FE39.	no
四字节字符的第一个字厄编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第二个字记编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39; 第三个字节编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第 四个字市编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39。 即 : 0x81308130 一 0x81308139; 0x81308230 一 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 一 0x8130FE39 ; 0x81318130 一 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c “0URo23061393 0xFE39FE30 一 0xFE39FE39 。	The first word of a four-byte character encodes in the range of 0x81 to 0xFE; The second word encoding range is 0x30 to 0x39; The third byte encodes in the range of 0x81 to 0xFE; The fourth character city code ranges from 0x30 to 0x39. i.e. : 0x81308130 a 0x81308139; 0x81308230 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 0x8130FE39; 0x81318130 a 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c "0URo23061393 0xFE39FE30 a 0xFE39FE39.	no
总体结构与码位范围分配见图 1 和表 1。	The overall structure and code range assignments are shown in Figure 1 and Table 1.	no
6 字符的排列顺序	6 The order in which the characters are arranged	no
6.1 单字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.1 The order in which characters are arranged by the brush part	no
单字记部分字符按照 GB/I 11383 一 1989 中相应字符的顺序排列 。	The characters of the word part are arranged in the order of the corresponding characters in GB/I 11383 to 1989.	no
6.2 双字市部分字符的排列顺序	6.2 The order in which the characters of the double-character city are arranged	no
双字下部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 A。	The order in which the characters under the double word are arranged should conform to Appendix A.	no
6.3 四字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.3 The order in which the characters of the four-character brush part are arranged	no
自 0x81308130 至 0x8439FE39 共 50400 个码位,对应双字节部分未包括的所有 GB/T 13000 基本多文种平面的字符,按照GB/T13000 基本多文种平面相应字符的顺序排列 。	A total of 50400 code points from 0x81308130 to 0x8439FE39, corresponding to all GB/T 13000 basic multilingual plane characters not included in the double-byte part, are arranged in the order of the corresponding characters of the GB/T13000 basic multilingual plane.	no
自 0x90308130 至 0xE339FE39 共 1058400 个码位用于对应 GB/T 13000 的16个辅助平面,字符排列顺序完全按照 GB/I 13000 的 16个辅助平面的相应码位顺序依次排列 。	A total of 1058400 code points from 0x90308130 to 0xE339FE39 are used to correspond to the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/T 13000, and the character arrangement order is exactly in the corresponding code point order of the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/I 13000.	no
四字节部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 C。	The four-byte partial character arrangement order should conform to Appendix C.	no

9.1 通则	9.1 General	yes
本文件规定三个实现级别。	This document specifies three levels of implementation.	yes
符合相应实现级别的系统软件产品,应提供相应实现级别范围内全部字符的输入输出功能。	System software products that conform to the corresponding implementation level shall provide input and output functions for all characters within the corresponding implementation level.	yes
9.2 实现级别 1	9.2 Implementation Level 1	yes
实现级别 1 文持本文件的单字节编码部分、双季节编码部分和四字下编玛部分的 CJK 统一汉字 ( 即 0x82358F33 一 0x82359636) 和 CJK 统一汉字扩A( 即 0x8139EE39 一 0x82358738) 。	Implement the CJK unified Chinese characters (i.e. 0x82358F33 一 0x82359636) and CJK unified Chinese character extensions (i.e. 0x8139EE39 一 0x82358738) of the single-byte encoded part, the double-season encoding part, and the four-character sub-encoded part of this document.	yes
任何本文件适用的产品均应满足实现级别 1 的要求。	Any product to which this document applies shall meet the requirements of implementation level 1.	yes
注: 根据软件应用需要 ,实现级别 1 还可选择文持表 3 列出的任何一种或多种非汉字文种。	Note: Depending on the needs of the software application, implementation level 1 can also choose any one or more of the non-Chinese characters listed in Table 3.	no
9.3 实现级别 2	9.3 Implement Level 2	no
实现级别 2 包含实现级别 1。	Implementation Level 2 contains Implementation Level 1.	no
此外 ,实现级别 2 还文持《通用 规范 汉字 表 }中的没有包合在实级别 1 之内的编码汉字。	In addition, implementation level 2 also holds encoded Chinese characters in the Common Specification Chinese Character Table } that are not encased within real level 1.	no
《 通用规范汉字表) 所收汉字在本文件中的代码位置和字形, 见附录下。	The code locations and glyphs of the Chinese characters included in this document are shown in the appendix.	no
系统软件及支撑软件,应满足实现级别 2 的要求 。	System software and supporting software should meet the requirements of implementation level 2.	no
注: 系统软件及文撑软件包括但不限于操作系统,数据库管理系统.中间件( 软件产品分类的信息见 GB/ 工 36475)。	Note: System software and supporting software include but are not limited to operating system, database management system. Middleware (see GB/36475 for information on software product classification).	no
9.4 实现级别 3	9.4 Implementation Level 3	no
实现级别 3 包含实现级别 2。	Implementation Level 3 contains Implementation Level 2.	no
此外,实现级别 3 还文持本文件规定的全部汉字及表 3 中的康黑部首。	In addition, implementation level 3 also holds all the kanji specified in this document and the Kanghei radicals in Table 3.	no
用于政务服务和公共服务的产品应满足实现级卉 3 的要求。	Products used in government services and public services should meet the requirements of Realization Level 3.	no
注: 政务服务和 共服务行业包括但不限于铁路运输业.道路运输业 \ 水上运输业.航空运输业、多式联运和运输代理业、邮政业、货币金融服、保险业、土地、管理业、卫生、国家机构、社会保障等 (行业分类的信息见 GB/ 工 4754)。	Note: Government services and common service industries include but are not limited to railway transportation. Road transport industry \ water transport industry. 描述 (DESCRIPTION) C 和 C++ 编译器是集成的.他们都要用四个步骤中的一个或多个处理输入文件: 预处理(preprocessing), Hii(compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking) .	DESCRIPTION C AND C++ COMPILERS ARE INTEGRATED. They all process the input file in one or more of four steps: preprocessing, Hii(compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking).	yes
源文件后级名标识源文件的语言, 但是对编译器来说, 后绥名控制着缺省设定:	The source file suffix identifies the language of the source file, but to the compiler, the suffix controls the default setting:	yes
gcc 认为预处理后的文件(.i) 是 c 文件, 并且设定 c 形式的连接，	GCC considers the preprocessed file (.i) to be a C file and sets the connection in the form of C.	yes
g++ 认为预处理后的文件 (.i) 是 c++ 文件 ,并且设定 c++ 形式的连接.	G++ considers the preprocessed file (.i) to be a C++ file and sets the connection in C++.	yes

除非使用了 -cec，-s, 或 -E 选项(或者编译错误阻止了完整的过程),否则连接总是最后的步骤.	Unless the -cec, -s, or -E options are used (or a compilation error prevents the complete process), the connection is always the last step.	no
在连接阶段中,所有对应于源程序的.e 文件，-1 库文件, 无法识别的文件名(包括指定的.o H 标文件和 .a 库文件)按命令行中的顺序传递给连接器选项 (OPTIONS)	During the connection phase, all .e files corresponding to the source program, -1 library files, unrecognized file names (including the specified .o H standard file and .a library file) are passed to the connector options (OPTIONS) in the order in the command line	no
选项必须分立给出 : de ' 完全不同于 `-d -r '.	The options must be given discretely : de ' is completely different from '-d -r '.	no
大多数 ` -=E :和 `-W' 选项有两个相反的格式 : -fname 和 -fno-name (或 -Wname 和 -Wno- name).	Most ' -=E : and '-W' options have two opposite formats: -fname and -fno-name (or -Wname and -Wno- name).	no
这里只列举不是默认选项的格式.	Only formats that are not default options are listed here.	no

明确指出后面输入文件的语言为 language (而不是从文件名后绥得到的默认选择).	Explicitly state that the language of the input file follows is language (not the default choice obtained from the filename).	yes
这个选项应用于后面所有的输入文件, 直到遇着下一个 `-x' 选项 .language 的可选	This option applies to all subsequent input files until the next '-x' option .language is available	yes

如果只操作四个阶段( 预处理, 编译, 汇编, 连接)中的一部分, 可以使用 ` -x' 选项 (或文件名后 Ah) 告诉 geo 从哪里开始,用 `~-c' ，`-s' ,或 `-E' 选项告诉 geo 到哪里结束.注意,某些选项组合 (例如 ，`-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c 编译或汇编源文件, ETER. ERA ATI 缺省情况下， GCC 通过用 ` .o' 蔡换源文件名后级 ` .ec 标文件名. 可以使用-o 选项选择其他名字.GCC忽略 -ec 选项后面任何无法识别的输入文伯 -S F 何事情.	If you are only operating some of the four stages (preprocessing, compiling, assembling, joining), you can use the '-x' option (or Ah after the filename) to tell geo where to start and '~-c', '-s', or '-E' to tell geo where to end. Note that some combinations of options (e.g. ,'-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c to compile or assemble source files, ETER. ERA ATI By default, GCC is replaced by '.o' for the source filename followed by the '.ec filename.' You can use the -o option to select a different name. GCC ignores any unrecognized input after the -ec option -S F Whatever.	yes
了的目标文件.	of the object file.	yes
编译后即停止, 不进行汇编件.	Stop after compilation, no assembly is made.	yes
在编译过程的不同阶段间使用管道而非临时文件进行工作, 因为那些系统的汇编器不能从管道读取数据，GNU 的汇编器没有这个问题，汇编器能够接受的 C "方言 ": 支持符合 ANSI 标准的 C 程序.	Work using pipes instead of temporary files between different stages of the compilation process, because the assemblers of those systems cannot read data from the pipes, GNU's assemblers do not have this problem, and the assembler can accept C "dialects": support for ANSI-compliant C programs.	yes
这样就会关闭 GNU Cc 中某些不兼容 ANSI Cc 的特性关键字, 以及诸如 unix 和 vax 这些表明当迎和极少使用的 ANSI trigraph 特性,以及禁上尽管使 用了(译注 :宿主环境 (hosted environment) 下所有的标准库可用，main 函数返回 一个 int 值, 典型例子是除了内核以外几乎所有的程序.对应的独立环境 (f£reestanding environment) 不存在标准库, 程序入口也不一定是 main, 最明显的例子就是操作系统内核.详情参考 gcc 网站最近的资料)	This would turn off some of the GNU Cc incompatible ANSI Cc feature keywords, as well as ANSI trigraph features such as unix and vax, which indicate that they are rarely used, and forbidden despite their use. The corresponding independent environment (f£reestanding environment) does not have a standard library, and the program entry is not necessarily main, the most obvious example is the operating system kernel. Please refer to the latest information on the GCC website for details)	yes
对于没有参数的函数声明, 例如 `int foo ();', 按 C 风格处理 --- 即不说明参数个数或类型. (仅针对 C++) .	For function declarations with no arguments, such as 'int foo(); ', treated in C style --- i.e. do not specify the number or type of parameters. (C++ only) .	no
正常情况下, 这样的函数 foo 在 C++ 中意味着参数为空.	Normally, such a function foo means that the argument is empty in C++.	no
节清单从这里删到试图支持传统 C 编译器的某些方面.	The list of sections is removed from here to attempts to support some aspects of the traditional C compiler.	no
详见NU c 手册,我们已经把细节删除, 这样当内容过时后, 人们也不会 HERI.	See the NUC manual for details, we've removed the details, so that when the content becomes outdated, people won't HERI.	no
除了一件事: 对于 c++ 程序 (不是C)，` -traditional' 选项带来一个附加效应,允许对 this 赋值.	Except for one thing: for C++ programs (not C), the '-traditional' option brings an additional effect that allows assignment to this.	no
他和`-Ethis-is-variable' 选项的果一样.	It has the same effect as the '-Ethis-is-variable' option.	no
-traditional-cpp 试图支持传统 Cc 预处理器的某些方面.	-traditional-cpp attempts to support some aspects of legacy CC preprocessors.	no
特别是上面提到有关预处理器的内容, 但是不包括 `-traditional' 选项的其他效应.	In particular, the above mentioned content about preprocessors, but does not include other effects of the '-traditional' option.	no
-fdollars-in-identifiers 允许在标识符 (identifier) 中使用 `$' 字符 (仅针对 C++) .	-fdollars-in-identifiers allows the '$' character in identifiers (C++ only).	no
你可以指定 `“-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' 选项显明禁止使用 `$' 符.	You can specify the '''-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' option to explicitly prohibit the use of the '$' character.	no
(GNU C++ 在某些目标系统缺省允许 `$' 符, 但不是所有系统.)	(GNU C++ allows the '$' character by default on some target systems, but not all.)	no
-fenum-int-equiv 允许 ant 类型到枚举类型 (enumeration) 的隐式转换 (MEF c++) .	-fenum-int-equiv allows implicit conversion of ant types to enumeration types (MEF c++).	no
正常情况下 GNU C++ 允许从 enum 到 int 的转换,反之则不行.	Normally, GNU C++ allows conversion from enum to int, but not vice versa.	no
-fexternal-—templates 为模板声明 (template declaration) 产生较小的代码 (仅限于 c++)，方法是对于每个模板函数 (template function),只在 定义他们的地方生成一个副本.	-fexternal-—templates produces smaller code (C++ only) for template declarations by generating only one copy of each template function where they are defined.	no
想要成功使用这个选项, 你必须在所有使用模板的文件中,标记`#pragma implementatio'(定义)或 `#Pragma interface'(声明).	To use this option successfully, you must mark '#pragma implementatio' or '#Pragma interface' in all files that use templates.	no
程序用 `-fexternal-templates ' 编译时, 模板实例 (template instantiation) 全部是外部类型.你必须让需要的实例在实现文件中出现.	When the program is compiled with '-fexternal-templates', template instantiation is all external types. You must have the required instances appear in the implementation file.	no
可以通过 typedef 实现这一点, 他引用所需的每个实例.	This can be achieved through typedef, which references each instance needed.	no
相对应的, 如果编译时使用缺省选项 ` -fno-exteznal-templates', 所有模板实例明确的设为内置.	Correspondingly, if the default option '-fno-exteznal-templates' is used when compiling, all template instances are explicitly set to built-in.	no
所有的成员函数(除了构造子函数和 mnew 或 delete 成员操作符) 视为所在类的虚函数.	All member functions (except constructors and the mnew or delete member operators) are treated as virtual functions of the class.	no
这不表明每次调用成员函数都将通过内部虚函数表.	This does not indicate that each call to a member function will pass through the internal virtual function table.	no
有些情况下, 编译器能够判断出可以直接调用某个虚函数; 这时就直接调用.	In some cases, the compiler can determine that a virtual function can be called directly; At this point, it is called directly.	no
-fcond-mismatch 允许条件表达式的第二和第三个参数的类型不匹配.	-fcond-mismatch allows the type of the second and third arguments of the conditional expression to not match.	no
这种表达式的值是 Void.-fthis-—is-variable 允许对 this 赋值 (仅对 c++).	The value of such an expression is void.-fthis--is-variable allows assignment to this (C++ only).	no
合并用户自定义的自由存储管理机制到 c++ 后,使可赋值的`this' 显得不合时宜.	Incorporating user-defined free storage management mechanisms into C++ makes the assignable 'this' seem out of place.	no
因此, 默认情况下, 类成员函数内部对 this 赋值是无效操作.	Therefore, by default, assigning a value to this inside a class member function is an invalid operation.	no
然而为了向后兼容, 你可以通过 `-fthis-is-variable' 选项使这种操作有效.	However, for backward compatibility, you can make this work via the '-fthis-is-variable' option.	no
-funsigned-char 把 char 定义为无符号类型,如同 unsigned char.	-funsigned-char defines char as an unsigned type, like unsigned char.	no
各种机器都有自己缺省的 char 类型. 既可能是 unsigned char 也可能是 signed char.	Each machine has its own default char type. It could be either unsigned char or signed char.	no
理想情况下, 当依赖于数据的符号性时, 一个可移植程序总是应该使用 signed char 或 unsigned chaz.	Ideally, a portable program should always use signed char or unsigned chaz when relying on the symbolism of data.	no
但是许多程序已经写成只用简单的 char, 并且期街这是有符号数(或者无符号数, 具体情况取决于编写程序的目标机器).	But many programs have been written with only simple char, and this is a signed number (or an unsigned number, depending on the target machine on which the program is written).	no
这个选项, 和它的反义选项, 使那样的程序工作在对应的默认值上.	This option, and its antisense option, makes such a program work on the corresponding defaults.	no
char 的类型始终应该明确定义为 signed char 或 unsigned char, 即使它表现的和其中之一完全一样.	The type of char should always be explicitly defined as signed char or unsigned char, even if it behaves exactly like one of them.	no
如果没有明确声明 ` signed' 或 "unsigned'修饰符, 这些选项用来定义有符号位域 (bitfield) 或无符号位域.	If the 'signed' or 'unsigned' modifier is not explicitly declared, these options are used to define either a signed bitfield or an unsigned bitfield.	no
缺省情况下,位域是有符号的, 因为他们继承的基本整数类型,如 int,是有符号数，然而, 如果指定了 `-traditional' 选项,位域永远是无符号数.	By default, bitfields are signed, because the basic integer types they inherit, such as int, are signed numbers, however, if the '-traditional' option is specified, the bitfields are always unsigned.	no
-fwritable-strings把字符串常量存储到可写数据段, 而且不做特别对待.	-fwritable-strings store string constants in writable data segments without special treatment.	no
这是为了兼容一些老程序,他们算改字符串常量是一个非常糟糕的想法、`-traditional' 选项也有相同效果.	This is a very bad idea for compatibility with some older programs that change string constants, and the '-traditional' option has the same effect.	no
执行摘要	Executive summary	yes
新冠肺炎对毒品市场的影响	The impact of coronavirus on the drug market	yes
其影响可能类似于2008年的经济危机	The impact could be similar to the 2008 economic crisis	yes
全球性的新冠肺炎疫情已使全世界陷入前所未有的危机。	The global coronavirus pandemic has plunged the world into an unprecedented crisis.	yes
在许多国家，这一疾病己使医疗服务机构穷于应付，几近崩溃，各国政府实施的限制措施已在全球经济中造成了严重紊乱。	In many countries, the disease has overwhelmed health services and nearly collapsed, and restrictions imposed by Governments have caused serious disruptions in the global economy.	yes
对于毒品市场，这场疫情的影响尚不清楚，也很难预测，但有可能影响深远。	For drug markets, the impact of the pandemic is unclear and difficult to predict, but it has the potential to be far-reaching.	yes
一些生产者可能会被迫寻找新的方法来制造毒品，因为限制流动的同时也限制了前体和基本化学品的获取。	Some producers may be forced to find new ways to manufacture drugs, as restrictions on movement also limit access to precursors and essential chemicals.	yes
贩运者由于旅行限制而无法越境，可能不得不寻找新的路线和方法。	Traffickers are unable to cross borders due to travel restrictions and may have to find new routes and methods.	yes
毒品使用和提供的模式可能会改变，政府的应对能力也可能会受到阻碍。	Patterns of drug use and provision may change, and governments' ability to respond may be hampered.	yes
新冠肺炎带来的转变是前所未有的，但还是可以从以往的危机中吸取一些经验教训。	The transformation brought about by COVID is unprecedented, but there are some lessons to be learned from previous crises.	yes
2008年经济危机后，一些吸毒者开始寻找更便宜的合成物质，使用模式转向注射毒品。	After the 2008 economic crisis, some drug users began looking for cheaper synthetic substances, and their use patterns shifted to injecting drugs.	no
与此同时，各国政府削减了与毒品相关的预算。	At the same time, governments have cut drug-related budgets.	no
如果各国政府以同样的方式应对当前的经济衰退，预防吸毒和相关风险行为等干预措施和戒毒治疗服务可能会受到沉重打击。	If governments respond in the same way to the current economic downturn, interventions such as drug use prevention and related risk behaviours and treatment services could be hit hard.	no
此外，拦截行动和国际合作的优先性可能会降低，使贩运者更容易行动。	In addition, interdiction operations and international cooperation may be given less priority, making it easier for traffickers to operate.	no
一些国家有大量毒品通过商业航班走私，预计这些国家的贩毒活动受到的直接影响最大。	Drug trafficking is expected to be most directly affected by large quantities of drugs smuggled through commercial flights in some countries.	no
有信使将甲基苯丙胺等合成毒品放在随身背包或藏在私人行李中携带，有时数量很大。由于几乎各地都对航空客运实施了限制，利用商业航空旅行供应毒品的活动可能会完全中断。	Messengers carry synthetic drugs such as methamphetamine in carry-on backpacks or hidden in personal luggage, sometimes in large quantities. With restrictions on air passenger transport imposed almost everywhere, the use of commercial air travel to supply drugs could be completely disrupted.	no
尽管国际邮政供应链也受到了干扰，但利用暗网和货物邮寄进行贩运的活动可能会增加。	While international postal supply chains have also been disrupted, the use of the dark web and the mailing of goods for trafficking is likely to increase.	no
从长远来看，经济衰退和相关的封闭措施可能会打乱毒品市场。	In the long run, the economic downturn and related lockdowns could disrupt the drug market.	no
由于不断上升的失业率和缺乏机会，贫困和弱势人群将更有可能以有害的方式吸毒，患上吸毒病症，并转向与毒品有关的非法活动一无论是生产还是运输。	As a result of rising unemployment and lack of opportunity, poor and vulnerable people will be more likely to use drugs in harmful ways, suffer from drug use disorders, and turn to illegal drug-related activities, whether produced or transported.	no
贩毒组织可能会利用这种情况，向脆弱人群提供服务，并招募新成员来壮大队伍。	Drug trafficking organizations may take advantage of this situation to provide services to vulnerable populations and recruit new members to grow their ranks.	no
随着政府应对能力的降低，这些转变可能会快速扎根，成为许多社区的新现实。	As governments become less able to respond, these shifts could quickly take root and become a new reality for many communities.	no
扩张与复杂性	Expansion and complexity	no
市场增长	Market growth	no
人口增长模式部分解释了市场扩张的原因	The population growth pattern partly explains the market expansion	no
世界各地的吸毒现象一直在增多，无论是从总体数字还是从吸毒者在世界人口中所占比例来看都是如此。	Drug abuse has been increasing around the world, both in terms of overall figures and the proportion of drug abusers in the world's population.	no
2009年估计吸毒者有2.1亿人，占全球15-64岁人口的4.8%,而2018年估计吸毒者有2.69亿人，占这类人口的5.3%。	An estimated 210 million drug users were in 2009, representing 4.8% of the global population aged 15-64, while in 2018 there were an estimated 269 million drug users, or 5.3% of this population.	no
在过去二十年期间，发展中国家吸毒情况的增长速度远远快于发达国家。	Over the past two decades, drug abuse in developing countries has grown much faster than in developed countries.	no
这在一定程度上反映了这一期间总体人口增长的差异、发达国家为7%,发展中国家为28%但也反映了发展中国家年 轻人口增长较快。	To some extent, this reflects the difference in overall population growth during this period, which was 7% in developed countries and 28% in developing countries, but also reflects the relatively rapid growth of young populations in developing countries.	no
青少年和年轻成年人在吸毒者中所占比例最大。	Adolescents and young adults make up the largest proportion of drug users.	no
在2000-2018年期间，发展中国家这一年龄段的人口增长了16%,而发达国家这一年龄段的人口减少了10%。	Between 2000 and 2018, the population in this age group grew by 16 per cent in developing countries, while it decreased by 10 per cent in developed countries.	no
1城市化是当前和未来毒品市场的一个驱动因素	1 Urbanization is a driver of current and future drug markets	no
无论是发达国家还是发展中国家，城市地区的吸毒情况都多于农村地区。	Drug abuse is higher in urban areas than in rural areas, in both developed and developing countries.	no
吸毒情况总体增多的部分原因是人口从农村向城镇的大规模流动一目前全世界人口有一半以上生活在城市地区，而1960年这一比例为34%。	The overall increase in drug abuse is partly due to large-scale rural-urban migrations—more than half of the world's population now lives in urban areas, up from 34 per cent in 1960.	no
城市化可能是毒品市场未来动态的一个关键因素，特别是在城市化趋势更为突出的发展中国家。	Urbanization could be a key factor in the future dynamics of the drug market, especially in developing countries where urbanization trends were more pronounced.	no
财富的增加与吸毒情况增多相联，但承受疾病负担最大的是最贫穷的人在世界范围内，发达国家的吸毒情况比发展中国家更为普遍。	Increases in wealth were associated with increased drug abuse, but the poorest people who bear the greatest burden of disease worldwide were more prevalent in developed countries than in developing countries.	no
可卡因之类的毒品更是与世界上较富裕的地区联系较为牢固。	Drugs such as cocaine are more strongly linked to wealthier parts of the world.	no
同样，在各国内部，社会富裕阶层的吸毒流行率较高。	Similarly, within countries, drug abuse prevalence is higher among the wealthier segments of society.	no
但转为吸毒病症的比率较高的却是社会经济地位较低的人。	However, the higher rates of conversion to drug use disorders are among people of lower socioeconomic status.	no
来自少数几个国家的数据表明，有害的吸毒模式与病症同低收入之间存在联系。	Data from a few countries indicate a link between harmful patterns of drug abuse and conditions and low income.	no
这些模式在较富裕的社会阶层似乎不太常见。	These patterns seem to be less common in wealthier social classes.	no
全球新冠肺炎危机造成的经济制约很可能会加剧包括吸毒者在内的最弱势群体的风险。	The economic constraints caused by the global coronavirus crisis are likely to exacerbate the risks for the most vulnerable, including drug users.	no
例如，劳动力市场的变化，如失业率上升，过去一直与吸毒情况的增加有关，而这场疫情己经迫使全球数千万人失业。	For example, changes in the labor market, such as rising unemployment, have been linked to an increase in drug use in the past, and the pandemic has forced tens of millions of people around the world to lose their jobs.	no
新冠肺炎或将导致毒品市场进一步扩张新冠肺炎的大流行可能会导致更多农民增加或从事非法作物种植，或是因为国家主管机关的控制能力降低，或是因为在经济危机之下可能有更多人不得不铤而走险，从事非法活动。	The pandemic may lead to more farmers growing illicit crops, either because the national authorities have less control over them, or because more people may have to take risks and engage in illegal activities during the economic crisis.	no
新冠肺炎的相关限制措施导致空中和陆路交通减少，海上贩运可能已经因此而增加，海上的拦截风险低，而且比空中或陆路走私的数量更多。	Coronavirus-related restrictions have reduced air and land traffic, and maritime trafficking may have increased as a result, with a low risk of interdiction at sea and more than smuggling by air or land.	no
最近已有报告称可卡因货物直接从南美经由海路运往欧洲。	There have recently been reports of cocaine shipments travelling directly from South America to Europe by sea.	no
复杂性增强	Increased complexity	yes
非国际管制物质的出现情况稳定，但有潜在危害的新型类阿片正在增多毒品市场正日趋复杂。	The emergence of non-internationally controlled substances is stable, but potentially harmful new opioids are increasing and the drug market is becoming increasingly complex.	yes
除大麻、可卡因和海洛因等植物类物质之外，已经增添了数百种合成毒品，其中许多并不在国际管制之下。药品的非医疗使用也快速增多。	In addition to plant-based substances such as cannabis, cocaine and heroin, hundreds of synthetic drugs have been added, many of which are not under international control. The non-medical use of pharmaceuticals is also increasing rapidly.	yes
会员国的国内市场每年约有500种新型活性物质。	The domestic market of Member States is about 500 new active substances per year.	yes
目前其中大多是兴奋剂，其次是合成的大麻素受体激动剂和少量的类阿片。	Most of these are currently stimulants, followed by synthetic cannabinoid receptor agonists and small amounts of opioids.	yes
虽然新型精神活性物质的总体数量已经稳定下来，但比例发生了变化。	While the overall number of new psychoactive substances has stabilized, the proportions have changed.	yes
在2014年确定的新型精神活性物质种类总数中，类阿片新型精神活性物质仅占2%,但到2018年，这一数字己上升至9%。	In 2014, opioids accounted for only 2% of the total number of new psychoactive substances identified, but by 2018 this figure had risen to 9%.	yes
类阿片新型精神活性物质中有许多是芬太尼的类似物，其药效和危害已得到证明，在北美导致了过量死亡事件，其他区域也有，但程度较轻。	Many of the new psychoactive substances in opioids are analogues of fentanyl, and their efficacy and harmfulness have been demonstrated, leading to overdose deaths in North America and, to a lesser extent, in other regions.	yes
在北美，芬太尼有的用作海洛因和其他毒品（包括可卡因和甲基苯丙胺）的掺杂剂，有的用来制造假冒的药用类阿片。	In North America, fentanyl is used either as a dopant for heroin and other drugs, including cocaine and methamphetamine, or in the manufacture of counterfeit medicinal opioids.	yes
一些证据表明，欧洲也有注射新型精神活性物质兴奋剂的现象：一项对欧洲六个城市废弃注射器残留物的研宄发现，许多注射器都沾有产生兴奋作用的新型精神活性物质》	There is some evidence that new psychoactive stimulants are also injected in Europe: a study of discarded syringe residues in six European cities found that many syringes were contaminated with new psychoactive substances that excitate their effects"	yes
2新型精神活性物质的使用可能会逐渐牢固存在于弱势群体中	2 The use of new psychoactive substances may gradually become firmly present among vulnerable groups	no
单一种类的新型精神活性物质几乎从未形成大的市场。	A single class of new psychoactive substances almost never forms a large market.	no
但来自欧洲的证据表明，合成大麻素在无家可归者和监狱囚犯等社会边缘群体中是一个严重的问题。	But evidence from Europe suggests that synthetic cannabinoids are a serious problem among socially marginalized groups such as homeless and prison inmates.	no
有22个国家报告了监狱中使用新型精神活性物质的情况，其中大多数国家将合成大麻素确定为主要挑战。	Twenty-two countries reported on the use of novel psychoactive substances in prisons, with most identifying synthetic cannabinoids as a major challenge.	no
对前体化学品的管制迫使制毒者进行创新最常作为前体用来合成苯丙胺、甲基苯丙胺和“摇头丸”等毒品的许多化学品已被置于国际管制之下。	The control of precursor chemicals had forced drug producers to innovate, and many of the chemicals most commonly used as precursors for the synthesis of drugs such as amphetamine, methamphetamine and "ecstasy" had been placed under international control.	no
贩毒者和制毒者一直在寻找替代品一不仅有管制较松的物质，还有专门为规避管制而设计的化学品，即所谓的“特制前体”。	Drug traffickers and producers have been looking for alternatives — not only loosely regulated substances, but also chemicals specifically designed to circumvent controls, so-called "purpose-built precursors".	no
旨在阻止新冠肺炎传播的限制性措施很可能使依赖前体化学品的制毒者受到进一步挤压。	Restrictive measures aimed at stopping the spread of the coronavirus are likely to further squeeze producers who rely on precursor chemicals.	no
来自墨西哥的证据表明，这已经成为 现实：据报告，2020年3月，从东亚进口的甲基苯丙胺前体短缺促使墨西哥和美国的甲基苯丙胺价格上涨。	Evidence from Mexico shows that this is already a reality: in March 2020, a reported shortage of methamphetamine precursors imported from East Asia drove higher methamphetamine prices in Mexico and the United States.	no
市场瞬息万变	The market is changing rapidly	no
合成药物在中亚和俄罗斯联邦取代阿片剂	Synthetic drugs replace opiates in Central Asia and the Russian Federation	no
中亚和俄罗斯联邦的阿片剂市场在2008年至2018年期间似乎发生了变化。	The opiate markets in Central Asia and the Russian Federation appear to have changed between 2008 and 2018.	no
俄罗斯联邦当局截获的阿片剂数量下降了约80%，同时因使用类阿片而接受治疗的人数大幅减少。	The number of opiates intercepted by the authorities of the Russian Federation had decreased by about 80 per cent, while the number of people receiving treatment for opioid use had dropped significantly.	no
但兴奋剂市场却似乎日渐兴旺。	But the doping market seems to be booming.	no
有证据表明，甲基苯丙胺和各种卡西酮，包括甲氧麻黄酮和 a - 吡咯烷基苯戊酮，现在俄罗斯毒品市场上随处可见。	There is evidence that methamphetamine and various cathinones, including methoxyephedrone and a-pyrrolidinylvalerone, are now ubiquitous on the Russian drug market.	no
俄罗斯当局报告称，最近查获的制造各种非法药物的秘密加工点数量急剧上升，在两年内翻了一番多，2018年增至152个加工点。	Russian authorities reported a sharp rise in the number of recently seized clandestine laboratories for the manufacture of various illicit drugs, more than doubling in two years, to 152 in 2018.	no
阿富汗和伊拉克甲基苯丙胺市场增长	The methamphetamine market is growing in Afghanistan and Iraq	no
早在2012年，对医院、监狱和其他机构人员的调查就已经揭示了甲基苯丙胺在伊拉克的重要性。	As early as 2012, surveys of personnel in hospitals, prisons and other institutions revealed the importance of methamphetamine in Iraq.	no
结晶甲基苯丙胺已经成为“芬乃他林”和曲马多之外又一种令人担忧的主要药物。	Crystalline methamphetamine has become a major cause for concern in addition to fenataline and tramadol.	no
2015年的一项研宄进一步证实了这些发现，吸毒者表示大麻比“芬乃他林”或甲基苯丙胺更难获得。	These findings were further confirmed by a 2015 study in which drug users said marijuana was harder to obtain than "fenataline" or methamphetamine.	no
最近，伊拉克当局发现了多个甲基苯丙胺加工点，麻管局已对伪麻黄碱制剂的大批进口表示关切一甲基苯丙胺加工点将这些制剂用作前体。	Recently, the Iraqi authorities had discovered a number of methamphetamine processing sites, and the Board had expressed concern about the large import of pseudoephedrine preparations by one methamphetamine processing site as a precursor.	no
在阿富汗，甲基苯丙胺制造似乎始于2014年。	In Afghanistan, methamphetamine manufacturing appears to have begun in 2014.	no
自那时起，甲基苯丙胺的缉获量一直在稳步上升。	Since then, methamphetamine seizures have been steadily increasing.	no
但2019年上半年的缉获量一^657公斤——与上一年相比大幅骤增。	However, seizures in the first half of 2019 amounted to one^657 kg – a significant increase compared to the previous year.	no
在其他国家大量缉获了据认为源自阿富汗的甲基苯丙胺，这也表明该国的产量正在迅速上升。	The large seizures of methamphetamine, believed to originate in Afghanistan, in other countries also indicate that production in that country is rising rapidly.	no
政策变化和变化趋势	Policy changes and trends	yes
非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域大多有大麻使用增多的趋势	Most jurisdictions where non-medical cannabis use has been legalized have a trend towards increased cannabis use	yes
加拿大、乌拉圭和美国的11个法域允许制造大麻产品供非医疗使用。	Eleven jurisdictions in Canada, Uruguay and the United States allow the manufacture of cannabis products for non-medical use.	yes
在其中多数法域，大麻使用自合法化以来有所增多，尽管在其他未将非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域也观察到了同样的趋势。	In most of these jurisdictions, cannabis use has increased since legalization, although the same trend has been observed in other jurisdictions that have not legalized the non-medical use of cannabis.	yes
在美国最早通过立法的两个州科罗拉多州和华盛顿州，成年人非医疗使用大麻的情况增加，特别是过去一个月以及每天或几乎每天使用的情况增多，自2012年起便已超过了全国平均水平。	In Colorado and Washington, the first two U.S. states to pass legislation, non-medical marijuana use by adults has increased, particularly in the past month and on a daily or near-daily basis, exceeding the national average since 2012.	yes
所有指标都显示，自2011年以来，乌拉圭的大麻使用情况有所增加，上月使用情况几乎翻了一番。	All indicators show an increase in cannabis use in Uruguay since 2011, with almost doubling last month.	yes
这表明增加的主要原因是经常和频繁使用大麻。	This suggests that the main reason for the increase is the regular and frequent use of cannabis.	yes
加拿大的短期数据也表明，2018年至2019年合法市场扩大的同时，使用量也在增加。	Canada's short-term data also shows that the legal market expanded in 2018-2019 as well as usage increased.	yes
然而，2019年仍有40%的大麻使用者靠非法来源获得某些产品。	However, 40% of cannabis users still obtained certain products from illegal sources in 2019.	yes
全球大麻药草缉获量暴跌的背后原因是大麻合法化？	The reason behind the collapse in global cannabis herb seizures is the legalization of cannabis?	yes
2018年，全球大麻药草缉获量降至20年来的最低水平，这是因为北美的缉获量下降，在过去10年中下降了 84%。	In 2018, global cannabis herb seizures fell to their lowest level in 20 years, due to a decline in seizures in North America, which has fallen by 84% over the past 10 years.	no
相比之下，同期世界其他地区的缉获量几乎翻了一番。缉获的模式表明，旨在放开大麻市场的政策在下降中发挥了关键作用。	In contrast, seizures in other parts of the world almost doubled during the same period. The pattern of seizures suggests that policies aimed at liberalizing the cannabis market played a key role in the decline.	no
对新型精神活性物质的监管似乎有遏制作用在国内对新型精神活性物质的监管效果仍然很难评估。	The regulation of new psychoactive substances appears to have a deterrent effect, and the effect of domestic regulation of new psychoactive substances is still difficult to assess.	no
一些对新型精神活性物质采用不同监管制度的国家显示出不同的新型精神活性物质使用流行率。	Some countries with different regulatory regimes for new psychoactive substances show different prevalence of new psychoactive substance use.	no
在另一些国家，通过国内立法后，新型精神活性物质使用情况有所减少。	In other countries, the adoption of domestic legislation has led to a decrease in the use of new psychoactive substances.	no
弱势群体面临合法和非法毒品市场的伤害用于疼痛管理和姑息治疗的药用类阿片主要在高收入国家提供止痛药在各区域分布不均。	Vulnerable groups face harm from both legal and illicit drug markets, and pharmaceutical opioids for pain management and palliative care are widely available in high-income countries and are unevenly distributed across regions.	no
2018年，所有可供医疗消费的药用类阿片中，90%以上在高收入国家。	In 2018, more than 90% of all medicinal opioids available for medical consumption were in high-income countries.	no
大约50%在北美，40%在欧洲，还有2%在大洋洲。	About 50% are in North America, 40% in Europe and 2% in Oceania.	no
这些国家的人口约占全球人口的12%。	These countries account for about 12% of the global population.	no
据估计，低收入和中等收入国家的人口占全球人口的88%,但消费的药用类阿片却不到10%。	It is estimated that low- and middle-income countries account for 88% of the global population but consume less than 10% of medicinal opioids.	no
获取药用类阿片的障碍与许多因素有关，包括立法、文化、卫生系统和处方做法。	Barriers to access to medicinal opioids are linked to many factors, including legislation, culture, health systems and prescribing practices.	no
较贫穷的人患吸毒病症的风险更大2018年约有3,560万人患有吸毒病症。	Poorer people are at greater risk of developing drug use disorders, with some 35.6 million people living with drug use disorders in 2018.	no
贫困、有限的教育和社会边缘化可能会增加吸毒病症风险，并加剧其后果。高收入国家的研宄证实了这一点，在这些研究中，个人不利的社会经济轨迹一不仅仅是他们在某一时间点的状况一也与吸毒病症风险有关。	Poverty, limited education and social marginalization can increase the risk of drug use disorders and exacerbate their consequences. This is confirmed by studies in high-income countries, where individuals' adverse socioeconomic trajectories are not only associated with their status at a certain point in time, but also with drug use risk disorders.	no
吸毒病症还会加深社会经济劣势，进一步增加失业、贫困和无家可归的风险，从而助长劣势的恶性循环。这些结果也可能与刑事司法系统内的侮辱性态度和后果有关。	Drug abuse also exacerbates socio-economic disadvantage and further increases the risk of unemployment, poverty and homelessness, thus contributing to a vicious circle of disadvantage. These results may also be related to humiliating attitudes and consequences within the criminal justice system.	no
妇女、少数民族和移民、性取向多样化群体、因武装冲突或灾难而流离失所的人以及农村环境中的人也可能受到吸毒病症的过重影响，或者在获得治疗服务方面遇到问题。	Women, ethnic minorities and migrants, sexually diverse groups, people displaced by armed conflict or disasters and people in rural settings may also be disproportionately affected by drug abuse or have problems accessing treatment services.	no
根据估计因残疾和过早死亡而损失的健康寿命年数的残疾调整寿命年（DALY)指标，在过去10年中，有害的吸毒对范围更广的社会影响加重。	According to the Disability-Adjusted Life Years (DALY) indicator, which estimates the number of years of healthy life lost due to disability and premature death, harmful drug use has exacerbated its wider social impact over the past 10 years.	no
2007年至2018年间，归因于吸毒的全球残疾调整寿命年数增加了 17%。	Between 2007 and 2018, the number of years of disability-adjusted life (DALYs) attributed to drug use increased by 17% globally.	no
注射吸毒者中常见的未经治疗的丙型肝炎导致的肝癌的相关残疾调整寿命年数增幅特别高——达到40%。	The increase in disability-adjusted life expectancy for liver cancer, which is common among injecting drug users, from untreated hepatitis C to liver cancer was particularly high – 40 per cent.	no
毒品和暴力之间的关系错综复杂很难确定精神活性物质的使用和暴力之间的所有因果关系。	The relationship between drugs and violence is complex, and it is difficult to establish all causal links between psychoactive substance use and violence.	no
全球范围的有限数据表明，迷醉可能是杀人的一个重要因素。	Limited data worldwide suggests that intoxication may be an important factor in homicide.	no
但在暴力事件中，酒精的作用似乎比毒品更大。	But alcohol appears to play a greater role than drugs in violent incidents.	no
虽然吸毒可能会导致犯罪，但在某些情况下，这种联系可以部分归因于多种中介因素，如社会经济劣势以及由个人风险、家庭环境和同龄人影响造成的其他类型的逆境。	While drug use can lead to crime, in some cases this link can be attributed in part to a variety of mediating factors, such as socioeconomic disadvantage and other types of adversity caused by personal risk, family environment, and peer influence.	no
贩毒和暴力之间的联系是多方面的。	The link between drug trafficking and violence is manifold.	no
如果已有稳定的犯罪结构，包括国际贩毒在内的大规模有组织犯罪活动有可能在无暴力的情况下实施。	If stable criminal structures exist, large-scale organized criminal activities, including international drug trafficking, are likely to be carried out without violence.	no
短期内，暴力的存在和程度与其说取决于贩运的数量，不如说取决于造成有组织犯罪集团之间力量平衡不稳定的某些变化，例如非法市场规模的变化，知名罪犯的死亡或监禁，以及使一个集团弱于另一个集团的执法措施。	In the short term, the existence and extent of violence depends not so much on the volume of trafficking as on certain changes that destabilize the balance of power between organized criminal groups, such as changes in the size of the illicit market, the death or imprisonment of well-known criminals, and law enforcement measures that make one group weaker than another.	no
最新趋势	Latest trends	yes
吸毒大麻是最常用的物质，类阿片危害最大	Drug marijuana is the most commonly used substance, and opioids are the most harmful	yes
据估计，2018年使用大麻的有 1.92 亿人，使之成为全球使用最多的毒品。	An estimated 192 million people used cannabis in 2018, making it the most used drug globally.	yes
相比之下，2018年使用类阿片的有5,800万人。	By comparison, 58 million people used opioids in 2018.	yes
但阿片类药物的相关危害却因使用者较少而受到忽视。	But the harms associated with opioids are overlooked by the fact that they are fewer users.	yes
在2017年与吸毒病症有关的估计167,000例死亡中，有66%是这类物质造成的，在据信为吸毒导致的残疾或过早死亡而损失的2,100万年寿命中，有50%是这类物质造成的。	Of the estimated 167,000 deaths related to drug use disorders in 2017, 66 percent were caused by these substances, and 50 percent of the 21 million life years believed to be lost for disability, or premature death from drug use.	yes
合成类阿片的非医疗使用加剧了公共卫生危机	The non-medical use of synthetic opioids has exacerbated the public health crisis	yes
在西非、中部非洲和北非，加剧类阿片危机的是曲马多；在北美则是芬太尼。这两个区域在经济、人口统计数据或一般吸毒模式方面几乎没有共同点，但都在奋力抗击由容易获得且生产成本低的物质助长的类阿片危机。	In West, Central and North Africa, it is tramadol that exacerbates the opioid crisis; In North America, it's fentanyl. The two regions have little in common economically, demographically, or general drug use patterns, but both struggle with the opioid crisis fuelled by readily available and low-cost substances.	yes
在北美，芬太尼等合成类阿片的使用导致了20年来类阿片过量致死人数增加。	In North America, the use of synthetic opioids such as fentanyl has led to a 20-year increase in opioid overdose deaths.	yes
2018年，在美国登记的67,367例过量死亡中，有三分之二涉及芬太尼。	In 2018, two-thirds of the 67,367 overdose deaths registered in the United States involved fentanyl.	yes
加拿大也报告了类似的结果，只是数字较低。	Canada reported similar results, albeit at lower numbers.	no

在西非、中部非洲和北非，非医疗用途曲马多的市场已有大幅增长。	In West, Central and North Africa, the market for tramadol for non-medical uses has grown substantially.	no
在该区域，接受治疗的曲马多使用病症患者越来越多。	In this region, an increasing number of patients are receiving treatment for tramadol use conditions.	no

但2018年，在印度通过一项监管曲马多的新法律之后，全球缉获量降至32吨。	But in 2018, after India passed a new law regulating tramadol, global seizures fell to 32 tons.	no
促成这两地危机的是制造简单和生产成本低，此外还有对曲马多和许多芬太尼类似物或其前体缺乏国际监管。	The crisis has contributed to the simplicity and low cost of production, as well as the lack of international regulation of tramadol and many fentanyl analogues or their precursors.	no
使这两地危机恶化的是这些物质在药品市场和非法市场上都有供应，因而更加难以发现和防止其滥用。	The crises in both regions are exacerbated by the availability of these substances on both drug and illicit markets, making it more difficult to detect and prevent their abuse.	no

在一些市场上，可卡因和甲基苯丙胺可以共存，有时是相互替代，这样一种药物的使用量上升时另一种药物的使用量就下降，有时是同时增加和减少以满足同一市场的需求。	In some markets, cocaine and methamphetamine can coexist, sometimes as substitutes for each other, so that the use of one drug increases and the use of the other decreases, sometimes increasing and decreasing at the same time to meet demand in the same market.	no

【环球时报驻比利时特派记者 牛瑞飞】据法新社2月10日报道，在当天最新的一次欧盟峰会上，欧盟委员会主席冯德莱恩表示，欧盟领导人同意就非法移民问题出台更严格的政策，以此更易于驱逐非法移民。	According to Agence France-Presse on February 10, at the latest EU summit on the same day, European Commission President von der Leyen said that EU leaders agreed to introduce stricter policies on illegal immigration to make it easier to deport illegal immigrants.	yes

然而，欧盟与各成员国就围栏费用支付等问题争吵不休。	However, the EU has squabbled with member states over issues such as the payment of fencing fees.	yes
冯德莱恩一再表示，欧盟资金不会支付相关费用。	Von der Leyen has repeatedly said that EU funds will not pay for them.	yes
但一些成员国的外交官员称，如果欧盟能分担外部边界沿线安装摄像头、瞭望塔和其他基础设施的部分，这将给各国腾出国家预算从而加快建设进程。	But diplomats in some member states say that if the EU can share the installation of cameras, watchtowers and other infrastructure along external borders, it will free up national budgets to speed up the construction process.	yes
欧洲Euractiv网站称，欧盟官员承认，难民接收过程每一步都存在瓶颈，有限的接收能力和成员国不堪重负的移民当局无法阻止难民在欧盟各国提交“无数”庇护申请，欧盟的难民接收系统处于近乎“永久性的危机”中。	EU officials acknowledge that there are bottlenecks at every step of the refugee reception process, that limited reception capacity and overwhelmed immigration authorities in member states cannot prevent refugees from submitting "myriad" asylum claims across the EU, and that the EU's refugee reception system is in a near-"permanent crisis".	yes
据欧盟委员会估计，欧盟的申根国家去年收到超92万份庇护申请，比前一年增加近半。	The European Commission estimates that the EU's Schengen countries received more than 920,000 asylum applications last year, nearly half more than the previous year.	yes

最近，美国对华“芯片战”大有升级之势——先是荷兰、日本两国在美国施压下，同意启动对华半导体制造设备出口的管制；后有外媒报道，美国政府正考虑切断美国供应商与华为公司之间的所有联系，禁止美国供应商向华为提供任何产品；拜登政府还准备公布一项行政命令，限制美国对敏感的中国科技行业的投资……2023年开年不久，美国在遏制中国半导体相关产业发展上就恶招不断。	Recently, the United States' "chip war" against China has greatly escalated - first, the Netherlands and Japan agreed to start the control of the export of semiconductor manufacturing equipment to China under pressure from the United States; Later, foreign media reported that the US government is considering cutting off all contact between US suppliers and Huawei, and prohibiting US suppliers from providing any products to Huawei; The Biden administration is also preparing to issue an executive order restricting U.S. investment in sensitive Chinese tech sectors... Soon after the beginning of 2023, the United States has continued to make vicious moves to curb the development of China's semiconductor-related industries.	yes
近年来，美国打击中国“芯”发展的动作从未停歇，一边精准打压对华半导体产供链，一边构建“去中国化”的半导体产业链联盟，图谋在先进半导体产业上彻底“甩开”中国。	In recent years, the United States has never stopped cracking down on the development of China's "core", while accurately suppressing the semiconductor production and supply chain in China, while building a "de-Chinese" semiconductor industry chain alliance, in an attempt to completely "shake off" China in the advanced semiconductor industry.	yes
无论是拉拢韩国建立“技术同盟”，还是与韩国、日本和中国台湾地区建立芯片“四方联盟”，亦或借由美日印澳“四边机制”“印太经济框架”等机制建立半导体产业链“小圈子”，美国通过把政治化、阵营化、武器化的手段引入半导体产业，企图搭建美国主导的封闭产供链循环，从而弥补其在芯片制造领域的短板，维护其在全球芯片产业的优势地位。	Whether it is to win over South Korea to establish a "technology alliance", or to establish a chip "quadripartite alliance" with South Korea, Japan and Taiwan, or to establish a "small circle" of the semiconductor industry chain through mechanisms such as the "quadrilateral mechanism" and "Indo-Pacific economic framework" of the United States, Japan, India and Australia, the United States introduces politicization, camp and weaponization into the semiconductor industry in an attempt to build a closed production and supply chain cycle led by the United States, thereby making up for its shortcomings in the field of chip manufacturing and maintaining its dominant position in the global chip industry.	yes

个人养老金理财产品终于上线了。	Personal pension financial products are finally online.	yes
2月10日，中国理财网发布首批个人养老金理财产品名单，工银理财、农银理财和中邮理财的7只个人养老金理财产品正式发售。	On February 10, China Wealth Management Network released the list of the first batch of personal pension wealth management products, and 7 personal pension wealth management products of ICBC Wealth Management, ABC Wealth Management and China Post Wealth Management were officially launched.	yes
至此，个人养老金账户的“货架”终于集齐个人养老金储蓄、个人养老金理财、个人养老金保险、个人养老金公募基金四类产品。	At this point, the "shelf" of individual pension accounts has finally collected four types of products: personal pension savings, personal pension financial management, personal pension insurance, and individual pension public funds.	yes
据介绍，首批个人养老金理财产品，全部为公募类净值型开放式产品，其中新发产品5只、存续产品2只，除1只产品为混合类产品外，其余6只产品均为固定收益类产品。	According to reports, the first batch of personal pension wealth management products are all public net worth open-ended products, including 5 new products and 2 existing products, except for 1 product is a mixed product, the remaining 6 products are fixed income products.	yes
北京青年报记者看到，5只新发产品中有4只来自工银理财，全部是固定收益类产品，最短持有期限分别为365天、540天、720天和1080天，对应的业绩比较基准(年化)分别为3.70 % - 4.20 % 、 4.10 % - 4.60 % 、 4.40 % - 4.90 % 、 5.25 % - 5.75 % 。	The reporter of Beijing Youth Daily saw that 4 of the 5 new products came from ICBC Wealth Management, all of which were fixed income products, with the shortest holding periods of 365 days, 540 days, 720 days and 1080 days, and the corresponding performance comparison benchmarks (annualized) were 3.70% - 4.20%, 4.10% - 4.60%, 4.40% - 4.90%, 5.25% - 5.75%.	yes
剩余一只新发产品是“邮银财富添颐·鸿锦最短持有1095 天 1 号 ” ， 也是固定收益类产品，2月10日开始募集，2月19日结束募集，风险等级为二级。	The remaining new product is "Postage Wealth Tianyi Hongjin Shortest Holding 1095 Days No. 1", which is also a fixed income product, which began to be raised on February 10 and ended on February 19, with a risk level of Level 2.	yes

去年11月银保监会制定了《商业银行和理财公司个人养老金业务管理暂行办法 》 。	In November last year, the China Banking and Insurance Regulatory Commission formulated the "Interim Measures for the Management of Individual Pension Business of Commercial Banks and Wealth Management Companies."	no
《办法》规定，参加人可以通过个人养老金资金账户购买个人养老储蓄、个人养老金理财产品、个人养老金保险产品、个人养老金公募基金产品等个人养老金产品。	The Measures stipulate that participants can purchase personal pension savings, personal pension wealth management products, individual pension insurance products, individual pension public fund products and other personal pension products through individual pension fund accounts.	no
随后，人社部、财政部、国家税务总局三部门发布通知，明确个人养老金制度在北京、天津，以及河北石家庄、雄安新区，山西晋城市等36个先行城市和地区启动实施。	Subsequently, the Ministry of Human Resources and Social Security, the Ministry of Finance and the State Administration of Taxation issued a notice clarifying that the individual pension system will be implemented in 36 pilot cities and regions, including Beijing and Tianjin, as well as Shijiazhuang, Xiong'an New Area and Jincheng City in Shanxi.	no
截至2022年底，个人养老金参加人数1954万人，缴费人数613万人，总缴费金额142亿元。	By the end of 2022, there were 19.54 million individual pension participants, 6.13 million contributors, and a total contribution amount of 14.2 billion yuan.	no
此前，参与试点的银行只上架了个人养老储蓄、个人养老金保险产品和个人养老金公募基金三类产品。	Previously, the banks participating in the pilot only listed three types of products: personal pension savings, individual pension insurance products and individual pension public funds.	no
如今，个人养老金理财产品也聚齐之后，投资者该如何选择？	Nowadays, after personal pension financial products are also gathered, how should investors choose?	no
交银理财产品研发部专家表示，相比其他个人养老金产品，试点阶段的养老理财产品和个人养老金理财产品均具有三方面的特点。	Experts from the R&D Department of BOCOM Wealth Management Products said that compared with other personal pension products, the pension wealth management products and personal pension wealth management products in the pilot stage have three characteristics.	no
一是稳健性，风险管理机制更加健全，投资策略和理念更为稳健，并实施非母行第三方独立托管。	The first is robustness, the risk management mechanism is more sound, the investment strategy and concept are more stable, and the implementation of third-party independent custody of the non-parent bank.	no
二是长期性，试点阶段养老理财产品的期限都在5年及以上，下一步发行的个人养老金理财产品，最短持有期原则上为1年，鼓励持有3年以上。	The second is long-term, the term of pension financial products in the pilot stage is 5 years and above, and the shortest holding period of personal pension financial products issued in the next step is 1 year in principle, and it is encouraged to hold for more than 3 years.	no
三是普惠性，产品购买门槛低，起购点一般为1元，有的低至0.01元，产品的托管费、管理费等费率更加优惠。	The third is inclusiveness, the product purchase threshold is low, the starting point is generally 1 yuan, some as low as 0.01 yuan, the product custody fee, management fee and other rates are more favorable.	no
专业人士指出，投资者要根据产品特点和自己的风险承受能力进行选择。	Professionals pointed out that investors should choose according to the characteristics of the product and their own risk tolerance.	no
个人养老金储蓄具有期限较长、利率较高、安全性高的特点，适合风险承受能力弱的人群；个人养老金保险产品重在保障，比较适合无法承担投资风险，可以接受稳定收益的人群；而个人养老金理财产品和公募基金产品不保本也不保收益，有一定投资风险，但预期收益较高，适合具备一定的金融知识、风险承担能力较高的人群。	Personal pension savings have the characteristics of long term, higher interest rate and high security, which is suitable for people with weak risk tolerance; Individual pension insurance products focus on protection, which is more suitable for people who cannot bear investment risks and can accept stable income; Personal pension financial products and public fund products do not guarantee capital or income, there are certain investment risks, but the expected returns are high, suitable for people with certain financial knowledge and high risk-bearing ability.	no

健身行业应摆脱信任危机-中新网	The fitness industry should get rid of the crisis of trust - Chinanews.com	yes
又一大型健身房“暴雷”？	Another big gym "Thunderstorm"?	yes
近日，知名健身机构中健健身会员维权问题引起社会关注。	Recently, the issue of protecting the rights of members of Zhongjian Fitness in well-known fitness institutions has attracted social attention.	yes
春节后不少会员发现自己所在门店没有正常营业，随后，关于该机构倒闭跑路的传闻引起会员恐慌，导致公安、人社部门介入。	After the Spring Festival, many members found that their stores were not operating normally, and subsequently, rumors about the collapse of the institution caused panic among members, leading to the intervention of public security and human resources and social security departments.	yes
最后，该机构相关负责人出面回应，承诺会努力保障好员工和会员的合法权益，风波才得以平息。	Finally, the relevant person in charge of the institution responded and promised to work hard to protect the legitimate rights and interests of employees and members, and the turmoil was calmed down.	yes
个别健身机构的部分门店出现经营问题，暂时关闭，消费者本可心平气和等待问题解决，为何不少会员的第一反应是“大事不妙”？	Some stores of some fitness institutions have business problems and are temporarily closed, consumers can be calm and wait for the problem to be solved, why is the first reaction of many members is "something is not good"?	yes
健身俱乐部会员维权风波背后，是行业信任危机的深层次问题。	Behind the storm of health club members' rights protection is the deep-seated problem of the industry's trust crisis.	yes
国内传统健身房普遍采取预付费模式，“赚用户不来的钱”是其发展的底层逻辑。	Domestic traditional gyms generally adopt a prepaid model, and "making money that users do not come" is the underlying logic of their development.	yes
通过预售会员卡获取现金流，不断开新店，看似能够循环往复，实则寅吃卯粮，无法形成稳定的盈利模式。	Obtaining cash flow through pre-selling membership cards and constantly opening new stores seems to be able to repeat itself, but in fact, it is impossible to form a stable profit model.	yes
健身房跑路等行业负面信息频频传出，对消费者信心造成强烈冲击。	Negative information in industries such as gym runs is frequently reported, which has a strong impact on consumer confidence.	yes
从市场前景看，健身房当然算得上是一门有“钱途”的好生意。	From the perspective of market prospects, gyms are certainly a good business with "money".	no
健身赛道虽然起起伏伏，但始终受到资本关注。	The fitness track, despite its ups and downs, has always received capital attention.	no
多项数据显示，文体消费等领域热度不断攀升，市场持续回暖。	A number of data show that the popularity of cultural and sports consumption and other fields continues to rise, and the market continues to recover.	no
具体到健身市场，随着居民生活水平稳步提高，健康生活理念深入人心，健身行业发展大有可为。	Specific to the fitness market, with the steady improvement of residents' living standards, the concept of healthy life is deeply rooted in the hearts of the people, and the development of the fitness industry is promising.	no
形势越是趋好，行业越需重视发展质量。	The better the situation, the more the industry needs to pay attention to the quality of development.	no
然而，个别机构对消费复苏后的健身市场盲目乐观，刚从危机中走出来，又吹响开疆拓土的号角，把融资资金一股脑投入新店建设上。	However, some institutions are blindly optimistic about the fitness market after the recovery of consumption, just came out of the crisis, and sounded the clarion call to open up territory, and invested financing funds in the construction of new stores.	no
不可否认，这几年受疫情影响，不少机构退出，行业重新洗牌，有实力的企业此时选择性地加大收购力度、重新布局，未尝不是新机遇。	It is undeniable that in recent years, affected by the epidemic, many institutions have withdrawn, the industry has been reshuffled, and powerful enterprises have selectively increased their acquisition efforts and rearranged at this time, which is not a new opportunity.	no
但是，健身市场发展要想进入良性循环，迈上行稳致远的康庄大道，行业就必须改变传统模式，改变经营策略。	However, if the development of the fitness market wants to enter a virtuous circle and move up the road of stability and long-term prosperity, the industry must change the traditional model and change the business strategy.	no
只有稳扎稳打，重新建立起消费者的信任度、安全感，才能真正赢得市场、赢得未来。	Only by steadily and steadily re-establishing consumers' trust and sense of security can we truly win the market and win the future.	no
相比大建新店抢占市场，健身行业当前更需要的是沉下心来优化服务，用高质量发展来稳住用户。	Compared with building new stores to seize the market, the fitness industry currently needs to sink down to optimize services and stabilize users with high-quality development.	no
首先，要靠服务留住用户。	First of all, rely on service to retain users.	no
健身房属于服务行业，其本质是坚持“用户导向”，要紧紧围绕用户需求，把经营重心放在服务提质升级上。	Gym belongs to the service industry, its essence is to adhere to "user orientation", to closely focus on user needs, to focus on service quality upgrade.	no
其次，要靠数字化转型提升用户体验。	Second, digital transformation is needed to improve user experience.	no
比如当下流行的互联网健身房模式，实现用户按次付费和场地自选。	For example, the popular Internet gym model realizes user pay-per-use and venue selection.	no
同时，身体数据、运动数据得以有效利用，还可以满足社交需求，实现从线上到线下完整的服务闭环。	At the same time, body data and exercise data can be effectively used, and social needs can be met to achieve a complete service closed loop from online to offline.	no
没有私教推销，没有巨额年卡，用户对健身机构“跑路”的担忧降低了，信任感也就提升了。	Without personal training sales, no huge annual passes, users' worries about the "running away" of fitness institutions are reduced, and trust is improved.	no
另外，还要积极探索多元业态。	In addition, we must actively explore diversified business formats.	no
如今，体育消费已经从单一服务走向场景消费，健身俱乐部有望成为消费新入口，围绕健身所需的运动补给和健身器械等周边产品或将成为新的盈利点，为消费者提供更丰富选择。	Nowadays, sports consumption has moved from a single service to scene consumption, fitness clubs are expected to become a new entrance to consumption, and peripheral products such as sports supplies and fitness equipment required for fitness may become new profit points, providing consumers with richer choices.	no

买贵退差价！	Buy expensive and return the difference!	yes
南京楼市再现“差价赔付”-中新网	Nanjing property market reproduces "price difference compensation"-Chinanews.com	yes
扬子晚报讯(记者 马祚波)扬子晚报/紫牛新闻记者10日在采访中发现，十余年未见的“保价协议”又重回了南京楼市，位于江北新区的一家楼盘宣称“差价赔付”，在交房前其他房源的优惠大于之前的折扣，开发商愿意为买房人换房并退还差价。	Yangtze Evening News (Reporter Ma Zuobo) Yangtze Evening News/Purple Cow News reporter found in an interview on the 10th that the "price insurance agreement" that has not been seen for more than ten years has returned to the Nanjing property market, and a real estate project located in Jiangbei New District claims that the "price difference compensation", before the handover of other listings, the discount is greater than the previous discount, and the developer is willing to change houses for buyers and refund the difference.	yes
“保价协议”条件可不少	There are quite a few conditions for a "price insurance agreement"	yes
这家位于江北新区的楼盘名为保利扬子萃云台，看房人孙先生告诉记者，他在上周末逛楼盘时发现了一则“声明”。	The property in Jiangbei New District is called Poly Yangzi Cuiyuntai, and Mr. Sun, a house watcher, told reporters that he found a "statement" while visiting the property last weekend.	yes
他发给记者的图片上显示，该楼盘的开发商承诺，凡是在2月1日-2月28日期间购买房源的，自双方签订买卖合同之日起至对应房源交付，若该项目其他房源的优惠折扣大于之前购房所享折扣的(限与该商品房属于同一户型、同一楼栋、同一单元、同一物业类型的其他未售商品房)，开发商可以为购房者换房并退还差价。	The picture he sent to reporters shows that the developer of the real estate promises that if the property is purchased between February 1 and February 28, from the date of signing the sales contract between the two parties to the delivery of the corresponding listing, if the discount of other listings in the project is greater than the discount enjoyed by the previous purchase (limited to other unsold commercial houses belonging to the same type, the same building, the same unit, and the same property type as the commercial house), the developer can exchange houses for the buyer and refund the difference.	yes
孙先生表示，置业顾问表示这其实就是一份“保价协议”，目的是让买家放心出手，不用担心开发企业降价促销，“现在就怕买完了它就降价了，去售楼处闹吧没时间，不闹的话也确实窝心”。	Mr. Sun said that the property consultant said that this is actually a "price insurance agreement", the purpose of which is to let buyers feel at ease, do not have to worry about the development company's price reduction promotion, "now I am afraid that after buying it, I will reduce the price, go to the sales office to make trouble, there is no time, if you do not make trouble, it is indeed comfortable."	yes
还有不少买房人则认为，“保价协议”虽然是在给购房者吃“定心丸”，不过条件却不低。	There are also many buyers who believe that although the "price insurance agreement" is giving buyers a "reassuring pill", the conditions are not low.	yes
打算在江北买一套刚需房的郑女士说，保价的房源首先是要同一户型，还得在同一楼栋、同一个单元，买家可以比价的房源寥寥，因此“门槛”还是蛮高的。	Ms. Zheng, who plans to buy a just-needed house in Jiangbei, said that the insured housing must first be the same type, but also in the same building and the same unit, and there are few houses that buyers can compare prices with, so the "threshold" is still quite high.	yes
也有购房者认为，由于信息不对称，销售时不排除给出额外的让利，买家“维权”的难度不小。	Some buyers believe that due to information asymmetry, additional concessions are not ruled out when selling, and it is not easy for buyers to "protect their rights".	yes
能否留住买房人有待观察	It remains to be seen whether it will be possible to retain buyers	no
记者在南京网上房地产上查询得知，该楼盘于去年11月首领两幢楼共计252套房源的销许，户型面积有105平方米、114平方米、129平方米等，全装修销许均价为39843元/㎡。	The reporter inquired on Nanjing online real estate and learned that the property was sold in November last year for a total of 252 houses in the two buildings, with a unit area of 105 square meters, 114 square meters, 129 square meters, etc., and the average price of full decoration sales was 39,843 yuan / ㎡.	no
不过两个多月过去，网上房地产显示目前该楼盘的未售总套数为157套，占比为62.3%，其中8号楼共计128套，未售套数达113套，7号楼的124套中也有44套未售，项目的总成交套数只有33套，占比仅为13%。	However, more than two months later, online real estate shows that the total number of unsold units in the property is currently 157 units, accounting for 62.3%, of which Building 8 has a total of 128 units, the number of unsold units reaches 113 sets, and 44 sets of 124 units in Building 7 are also unsold, and the total number of completed units of the project is only 33 sets, accounting for only 13%.	no
市场人士介绍，“保价协议”在2008年也曾在南京出现过。	According to market sources, the "price insurance agreement" also appeared in Nanjing in 2008.	no
当年8月份，河西黄山路上的楼盘横塘西苑为了吸引买房人眼球，推出了《保价计划》，具体内容为“公司郑重承诺，若一年内项目优惠幅度扩大，由此产生的差额，公司将按差额退还给老业主”。	In August of that year, Hengtang Xiyuan, a real estate project on Huangshan Road in Hexi, launched the "Price Insurance Plan" in order to attract the attention of buyers, the specific content of which was "the company solemnly promises that if the preferential range of the project is expanded within one year, the company will refund the difference to the old owner according to the difference".	no
此后2011年4月，南京也有9家楼盘拿出部分房源承诺“差价赔付”。	Since then, in April 2011, 9 real estate projects in Nanjing have taken out some listings and promised to "pay the difference".	no
“楼市在回暖，此时更需要一针‘强心剂’。	"The property market is picking up, and at this time, a 'booster' is needed.	no
”南京地产行业一位资深操盘手沈先生表示，“保价协议”也是房企的营销方式之一。	Mr. Shen, a senior trader in Nanjing's real estate industry, said that the "price insurance agreement" is also one of the marketing methods of real estate enterprises.	no
他认为如今开发企业比买房人更需要信心，推出“保价协议”其实也是在给其打气。	He believes that developers need confidence more than buyers, and the introduction of "price insurance agreements" is actually encouraging them.	no
至于能否留住买房人，他表示这取决于调控政策、贷款门槛等多重因素的影响，就目前来看仍有待观察。	As for whether it can retain buyers, he said that it depends on the impact of multiple factors such as regulatory policies and loan thresholds, and it remains to be seen for now.	no
多项数据衰退 台湾经济开年表现不佳-中新网	A number of data recession Taiwan's economy began the year with poor performance-Chinanews.com	yes
新华社台北2月11日电(记者赵博、黄扬)出口贸易额“连五黑”，制造业采购经理人指数(PMI)连续7个月紧缩，消费者物价指数(CPI)又见“3字头”……近期，台湾当局陆续发布2023年1月经济数据。	Taipei, Feb. 11 (Xinhua) -- Export trade volume is "five blacks", the manufacturing purchasing managers' index (PMI) has tightened for seven consecutive months, and the consumer price index (CPI) has seen "three characters"... Recently, the Taiwan authorities have successively released economic data for January 2023.	yes
专家分析认为，台湾经济开年表现欠佳，增长压力不小。	According to expert analysis, Taiwan's economy began the year with poor performance and growth pressure was not small.	yes
据台当局财政事务主管部门公布，台湾地区今年1月出口315.1亿美元，年减21.2%，连续第5个月负增长。	According to the financial affairs department of the Taiwan authorities, Taiwan's exports in January this year amounted to $31.51 billion, down 21.2 percent year-on-year, marking the fifth consecutive month of negative growth.	yes
11项主要出口货类的出口额与去年同期相比，均出现衰退。	Exports of 11 major export categories declined compared to the same period last year.	yes
塑橡胶及其制品、光学器材跌幅最深，分别年减37.6%、35.7%。	Plastic rubber and its products and optical equipment fell the most, down 37.6% and 35.7% respectively.	yes
电子零组件出口年减20.1%，创11年来最大减幅。	Exports of electronic components fell by 20.1% year-on-year, the largest decline in 11 years.	yes
其中，集成电路年减18.3%，创14年来最大跌势。	Among them, integrated circuits decreased by 18.3% year-on-year, the largest decline in 14 years.	yes
该部门统计处长蔡美娜表示，这显示消费性电子产业需求疲弱效应扩散，电子产业进入修正期。	Cai Meina, director of the department's statistics department, said that this shows that the weak demand effect of the consumer electronics industry has spread, and the electronics industry has entered a correction period.	yes
统计显示，1月台湾地区进出口双降，出超金额仅23.4亿美元，创近3年来最低水平。	Statistics show that Taiwan's imports and exports fell in January, with an excess of only US$2.34 billion, the lowest level in nearly three years.	yes
台当局财政事务主管部门认为，全球终端需求减少，产业调整库存抑制厂商购料意愿，出口颓势短期难见改善，台湾今年首季出口衰退恐高于预期。	The financial affairs department of the Taiwan authorities believes that the global terminal demand has decreased, the industrial adjustment of inventories has inhibited manufacturers' willingness to buy materials, and it is difficult to see an improvement in the short-term export decline, and Taiwan's export recession in the first quarter of this year may be higher than expected.	no
据台湾中华经济研究院发布，今年1月台湾制造业采购经理人指数(PMI)经季节调整后为40.4%，较去年12月续跌3.3个百分点，连续7个月紧缩。	According to Taiwan's Chung Hua Institute of Economic Research, Taiwan's manufacturing purchasing managers' index (PMI) in January this year was 40.4% seasonally adjusted, down 3.3 percentage points from December last year, tightening for seven consecutive months.	no
经济监测指标体系中，PMI以50%为荣枯线，指数大于50%，代表景气扩张，反之为紧缩。	In the economic monitoring index system, the PMI is 50% as the glory and dry line, and the index is greater than 50%, which represents economic expansion, and vice versa.	no
1月台湾PMI五项组成指标中，新增订单、生产与人力雇佣紧缩，供应商交货时间下降，存货紧缩。	Among the five components of Taiwan's PMI in January, new orders, production and labor employment tightened, supplier delivery times declined, and inventories tightened.	no
六大产业全数回报PMI紧缩，各产业依紧缩速度排序为电力暨机械设备产业(35.1%)、电子暨光学产业(35.2%)、化学暨生技医疗产业(39.2%)、基础原物料产业(42.4%)、交通工具产业(42.6%)与食品暨纺织产业(45.7%)。	All six major industries reported PMI contraction, with the power and machinery and equipment industry (35.1%), electronics and optical industry (35.2%), chemical and biotechnology medical industry (39.2%), basic raw materials industry (42.4%), transportation industry (42.6%) and food and textile industry (45.7%) in order of tightening rate.	no
物价方面，台当局“主计总处”公布，今年1月台湾CPI年增率为3.04%，自去年7月以来再度冲破3%。	In terms of prices, the "Comptroller's Office" of the Taiwan authorities announced that the annual growth rate of Taiwan's CPI in January this year was 3.04%, and it has broken through 3% again since July last year.	no
其中，蔬菜价格飞涨28.25%，创17个月新高。	Among them, vegetable prices soared 28.25%, hitting a 17-month high.	no
台“主计总处”专门委员曹志弘坦言，菜价涨幅确实超乎预期，排除春节因素，今年1月和2月平均CPI应接近去年12月的2.71%，通胀压力还是存在，且仍在高点。	Cao Zhihong, a special member of Taiwan's "General Accounting Office", said frankly that the price increase in vegetable prices did exceed expectations, excluding the Spring Festival factor, the average CPI in January and February this year should be close to 2.71% in December last year, and inflationary pressure still exists and is still at a high point.	no
展望今年台湾经济，综合《联合报》、“Yahoo财经”等岛内媒体报道，专家表示悲观。	Looking forward to Taiwan's economy this year, experts expressed pessimism based on media reports on the island such as Lianhe Pao and Yahoo Finance.	no
台“中央大学”经济系教授吴大任分析，出口衰退可能造成出口制造业厂商现金流出现问题，债务违约风险上升。	Wu Daren, a professor at the Department of Economics of Taiwan's "Central University", analyzed that the export recession may cause cash flow problems for export manufacturing manufacturers, and the risk of debt default will increase.	no
同时，订单减少导致厂商削减人力成本，影响劳动市场和家庭经济，反过来冲击消费能力。	At the same time, the reduction in orders has led manufacturers to cut labor costs, affecting the labor market and household economy, which in turn affects consumption capacity.	no
台湾经济研究院研究员邱达生认为，今年欧美通胀状况未解，需求持续萎缩，预估台湾出口衰退会延续到上半年。	Chiu Tat-seng, a researcher at the Taiwan Institute of Economic Research, believes that this year's inflation situation in Europe and the United States is unresolved, demand continues to shrink, and it is expected that Taiwan's export recession will continue to the first half of the year.	no
由于台湾经济靠出口支撑，受出口低迷影响，全年经济增长表现将不如去年。	As Taiwan's economy is supported by exports, due to the impact of sluggish exports, the annual economic growth performance will not be as good as last year.	no
“全球复苏的重要引擎”-中新网	"An important engine of global recovery" - Chinanews.com	yes
“应对新冠疫情冲击，中国经济展现出了强大韧性。	"In response to the impact of the new crown epidemic, China's economy has shown strong resilience.	yes
近期市场预期表明，国际社会普遍看好中国未来发展。	Recent market expectations show that the international community is generally optimistic about China's future development.	yes
”西班牙知名中国问题专家、中国政策观察网名誉顾问胡里奥·里奥斯日前接受本报记者采访时表示，当前中国疫情防控进入新阶段，经济社会发展活力将进一步得到释放。	Julio Ríos, a well-known Spanish expert on China and honorary advisor of China Policy Observation Network, said in an interview with this reporter a few days ago that China's epidemic prevention and control has entered a new stage, and the vitality of economic and social development will be further released.	yes
里奥斯表示，面对各种超预期因素冲击，中国以非凡的经济治理经验和措施沉着应对，充分体现出其经济韧性和管理水平。	Rios said that in the face of various unexpected factors, China has calmly responded with extraordinary economic governance experience and measures, fully demonstrating its economic resilience and management level.	yes

中新网北京2月11日电 (门睿)近日发布的《2022中国海归就业调查报告》(下称“报告”)显示，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高，我国企业对海外人才的需求亦呈上扬态势。	Beijing, Feb. 11 (Menrui) -- According to the "2022 China Returnee Employment Survey Report" (hereinafter referred to as the "Report") recently released, the scale of fresh international students in 2022 increased by 8.6% year-on-year, the number of international students returning to China to seek employment reached a new high, and the demand for overseas talents by Chinese enterprises also showed an upward trend.	yes
报告指出，自2020年以来，在中国国内求职的海归数量明显增长，回国求职的应届留学生数量增多。	The report points out that since 2020, the number of returnees seeking employment in China has increased significantly, and the number of fresh international students returning to China to seek employment has increased.	yes
与2021年相比，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高。	Compared with 2021, the scale of fresh international students in 2022 increased by 8.6% year-on-year, and the number of international students returning to China to seek employment reached a new high.	yes
从回国求职留学生的留学国家分布来看，英国占比最高，为41.4%，其次是澳大利亚(20.3%)和美国(9%)，排名与2021年一致。	From the distribution of study countries for returning international students, the UK accounted for the highest proportion at 41.4%, followed by Australia (20.3%) and the United States (9%), ranking in line with 2021.	yes
从同比增速来看，2022年来自马来西亚、日本、新加坡的应届留学生人数同比大幅上升，增速分别为66.1%、50.9%和37.7%。	From the perspective of year-on-year growth, the number of fresh international students from Malaysia, Japan and Singapore in 2022 increased sharply year-on-year, with growth rates of 66.1%, 50.9% and 37.7% respectively.	yes
来自加拿大、德国、美国、澳大利亚的应届留学生人数同比下降。	The number of fresh international students from Canada, Germany, the United States and Australia decreased year-on-year.	yes
2023春节后第一周海归人才供需走势 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	Supply and demand trend of returnee talents in the first week after the Spring Festival in 2023 Source: "2022 China Returnee Employment Survey Report"	yes

河南省规范整合口腔种植医疗服务价格-中新网	Henan Province standardizes the integration of oral implant medical service prices-Zhongxin.com	yes
央视网消息：种植牙是很多缺牙患者的理想选择，但一直以来，动辄上万元一颗的价格让很多患者望而却步。	CCTV News: Dental implants are the ideal choice for many patients with missing teeth, but for a long time, the price of tens of thousands of yuan has made many patients prohibitive.	yes
今年以来，随着种植牙集采的加速落地，各地也将种植牙降价提上日程。	Since the beginning of this year, with the acceleration of dental implant procurement, all localities have also put the price reduction of dental implants on the agenda.	yes
从2月10日起，河南省单颗常规种植牙医疗服务价格全流程调控目标为4300元，单颗常规种植全流程费用不高于调控目标的97%。	From February 10, the price of a single conventional dental implant in Henan Province is 4,300 yuan, and the cost of the whole process of a single conventional implant is not higher than 97% of the control target.	yes
种植牙齿指的是一种以植入骨组织内的下部结构为基础来支持、固位上部牙修复体的缺牙修复方式。	Dental implants refer to a type of missing tooth restoration that supports and holds the upper dental restoration based on the lower structure implanted in bone tissue.	yes
记者从郑州大学第一附属医院了解到，以单颗常规种植为例，从种植到最后修复，价格大概要一万六七千元左右。	The reporter learned from the First Affiliated Hospital of Zhengzhou University that taking a single conventional planting as an example, from planting to final restoration, the price is about 16,700 yuan.	yes
患者 何莹：新政策之后，大夫跟我说，像我这种情况差不多就是8000多元、不到1万元，基本上能省一半。	Patient He Ying: After the new policy, the doctor told me that in my case, it is almost 8,000 yuan, less than 10,000 yuan, which can basically save half.	yes
在现行项目基础上，河南省还整合确定了“种植体植入费(单颗)”等15个口腔种植类医疗服务价格项目，并统一制定省管公立医疗机构价格和医保支付类别，取消或调整了牙种植体植入术等20个医疗服务价格项目。	On the basis of the current project, Henan Province has also integrated and determined 15 oral implant medical service price items such as "implant implant fee (single)", and unified the price and medical insurance payment categories of provincially managed public medical institutions, and cancelled or adjusted 20 medical service price items such as dental implant implantation.	yes
郑州市医疗保障局医药价格和招标采购处处长 李云杰：受益的主要是四方，一个是医保，医保的支出少了；医院的占压少了，病人会适当增加；对供应商来说得到了一个市场；对我们患者来说是得利最大的一方，植一颗牙的费用可能要减半甚至更多。	Li Yunjie, Director of the Pharmaceutical Price and Bidding and Procurement Department of Zhengzhou Medical Security Bureau: The main beneficiaries are the four parties, one is medical insurance, and the expenditure on medical insurance is less; The pressure in the hospital is less, and the number of patients will increase appropriately; A market is obtained for suppliers; For our patients, the most beneficial party, the cost of a dental implant may be halved or even more.	yes

制定公共场所无线局域网(WLAN)服务规范，推动全市各区人员密集和信息消费需求集中区域WLAN升级，提供千兆接入能力。	Formulate wireless local area network (WLAN) service specifications in public places, promote WLAN upgrades in areas with dense personnel and concentrated information consumption demand in all districts of the city, and provide gigabit access capabilities.	yes
