近年来，既有刘畊宏、东方甄选等现象级大V，也有在垂直细分领域出现的不少非大众所知的达人和商家，他们通过持续打造符合自己品牌调性的优质内容，提升长期经营效益。	In recent years, there are not only phenomenal big Vs such as Liu Genghong and Oriental Selection, but also many unknown experts and merchants in vertical segments, who continue to create high-quality content in line with their own brand tonality to improve long-term business efficiency.	no
抖音电商明星作者运营负责人高亚轩介绍，过去一年有627万创作者通过抖音电商将内容变现，他们的内容创作量增长了252%，总成交额也翻了一倍以上。	Gao Yaxuan, head of Douyin e-commerce star author operations, said that 6.27 million creators have monetized their content through Douyin e-commerce in the past year, and their content creation has increased by 252%, and the total turnover has more than doubled.	no
“在这些数字背后，我们能感受到一个蓬勃生长、具有旺盛生命力的作者生态。	"Behind these numbers, we can feel a thriving and vigorous author ecology.	no
”高亚轩说。	Gao Yaxuan said.	no
北京师范大学传播创新与未来媒体实验平台此前发布了《电商行业内容生态健康指数(ECHI)报告》，从数据维度解析了当前电商行业中“新变量”——优质内容的重要性，运用指数对国内27家主流电商平台内容生态情况进行了评估。	The Communication Innovation and Future Media Experimental Platform of Beijing Normal University previously released the "E-commerce Industry Content Ecological Health Index (ECHI) Report", which analyzed the importance of high-quality content, the "new variable" in the current e-commerce industry, from the data dimension, and used the index to evaluate the content ecology of 27 mainstream e-commerce platforms in China.	no
根据上述报告的电商行业内容生态健康指数排名，抖音电商、快手、淘宝、拼多多、京东位居前五。	According to the content ecological health index ranking of the e-commerce industry in the above report, Douyin e-commerce, Kuaishou, Taobao, Pinduoduo, and JD.com ranked in the top five.	no
报告认为，电商行业内容生态是一个综合性概念，是将电商与内容进行整合，但并非所有内容都可与电商整合，好的PGC(专业生产内容)与UGC(用户原创内容)才是与电商进行整合的优质载体，内容平台价值越高，消费与推广的场景也就越来越丰富，电商植入的可能性也就越高，商业价值也就越强，这种公共领域和私人领域逐步集成分布的电商内容生产和内容消费的比例也就会越高。	The report believes that the content ecology of the e-commerce industry is a comprehensive concept, is to integrate e-commerce and content, but not all content can be integrated with e-commerce, good PGC (professionally produced content) and UGC (user-generated content) is a high-quality carrier for integration with e-commerce, the higher the value of the content platform, the richer the consumption and promotion scenarios, the higher the possibility of e-commerce implantation, the stronger the commercial value. The proportion of e-commerce content production and content consumption that is gradually integrated and distributed between the public and private sectors will be higher.	no
现场，北京师范大学新闻传播学院教授、中国传媒经济与管理专业委员会理事长喻国明对《报告》做了分析解读。	At the scene, Yu Guoming, professor of the School of Journalism and Communication of Beijing Normal University and chairman of the China Media Economics and Management Professional Committee, analyzed and interpreted the Report.	no
他表示，就内容价值而言，当前电商行业已经从“消费可及性”过渡到“消费品质化”阶段，优质、专业、差异化的内容是电商行业的“硬通货”。	He said that in terms of content value, the current e-commerce industry has transitioned from "consumption accessibility" to "consumption quality" stage, and high-quality, professional and differentiated content is the "hard currency" of the e-commerce industry.	no
同时，内容成为电商发展新阶段的根本和抓手，知识付费、专业性知识、KOL(关键意见领袖)等PGC内容开始在电商直播中成为标配。	At the same time, content has become the foundation and starting point for the new stage of e-commerce development, and PGC content such as knowledge payment, professional knowledge, and KOLs (key opinion leaders) have begun to become standard in e-commerce live broadcasts.	no
展望电商行业的未来发展，喻国明提出两方面的建议。	Looking forward to the future development of the e-commerce industry, Yu Guoming put forward two suggestions.	no
一个是从内容结构提升的角度看，推动电商内容生态健康程度和质量整体提升，打造正向内容创作和管理标准，实现电商行业内容生态健康系统指数与动态均衡。	One is to promote the overall improvement of the health and quality of e-commerce content ecology from the perspective of content structure improvement, create positive content creation and management standards, and achieve the content ecological health system index and dynamic balance of the e-commerce industry.	no
另一个是从外部生态看，要实现内容电商行业的健康发展和外部环境的价值协同与共创。	The other is from the perspective of the external ecology, to achieve the healthy development of the content e-commerce industry and the value synergy and co-creation of the external environment.	no
“未来电商行业还需要更多的数据、人工智能方面的支持，形成对未来发展稳定性的预测；此外，为商家提供更规范、健康的成长空间，实现电商行业中企业、用户、产品与服务的价值协同，共创健康内容生态。	"In the future, the e-commerce industry will need more data and artificial intelligence support to form a prediction of future development stability; In addition, it provides merchants with more standardized and healthy growth space, realizes the value synergy of enterprises, users, products and services in the e-commerce industry, and creates a healthy content ecology.	no
”(完)	(End)	no
北交所融资融券交易业务下周启动-中新网	BSE margin trading business to start next week-Chinanews.com	yes
本报讯(记者 孙杰)昨晚，北交所发布消息，经中国证监会批准，北京证券交易所融资融券交易业务将于2月13日正式启动，届时已取得北交所融资融券交易权限的证券公司可接受投资者委托，向北交所进行融资融券交易申报。	Last night, the Beijing Stock Exchange released news that with the approval of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, the margin trading business of the Beijing Stock Exchange will be officially launched on February 13, when securities companies that have obtained the trading authority of margin trading on the Beijing Stock Exchange can accept the entrustment of investors to declare margin trading and securities trading to the Beijing Stock Exchange.	yes
首批56只融资融券标的股票名单以2023年1月31日为计算基准日确定。	The list of the first batch of 56 margin trading target stocks is determined on January 31, 2023 as the calculation base date.	yes
北交所表示，融资融券标的股票名单和可充抵保证金证券名单将通过北交所官网的“信息披露-融资融券信息”栏目公布，方便投资者查询。	According to the BSE, the list of stocks subject to margin lending and the list of securities that can be covered with margin will be announced through the "Information Disclosure - Margin Lending Information" column on the official website of the BSE to facilitate investors' inquiries.	yes
融资融券是证券市场重要的基础性制度，也是国际证券市场中较为成熟的交易方式。	Margin trading is an important basic system in the securities market and a relatively mature trading method in the international securities market.	yes
去年9月2日，在宣布设立一周年之际，北交所对融资融券业务公开征求意见。	On September 2 last year, on the occasion of the first anniversary of its establishment, the Beijing Stock Exchange publicly solicited opinions on margin trading and securities lending.	yes
北交所融资融券交易的启动是持续推进北交所市场制度建设、完善交易机制、提升二级市场定价功能的重要举措。	The launch of margin trading on the BSE is an important measure to continuously promote the construction of the BSE market system, improve the trading mechanism, and improve the pricing function of the secondary market.	yes
融资融券制度有利于丰富投资者交易策略，满足投资者多元交易需求，促进市场价格发现，进一步提升市场流动性。	The margin trading system is conducive to enriching investors' trading strategies, meeting investors' diversified trading needs, promoting market price discovery, and further enhancing market liquidity.	yes
下一步，北交所将在中国证监会的领导下，持续做好融资融券业务各项保障工作，以投资者需求为导向丰富交易制度工具，完善相关配套机制，着力打造服务创新型中小企业的一流交易所。	In the next step, under the leadership of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, the Beijing Stock Exchange will continue to do a good job in guaranteeing margin trading and securities lending, enrich trading system tools guided by investor needs, improve relevant supporting mechanisms, and strive to build a first-class exchange serving innovative small and medium-sized enterprises.	yes

处理好守正与创新的关系，既要守好中国式现代化的本和源、根和魂，毫不动摇坚持中国式现代化的中国特色、本质要求、重大原则，确保中国式现代化的正确方向，又要把创新摆在国家发展全局的突出位置，顺应时代发展要求，着眼于解决重大理论和实践问题，积极识变应变求变，大力推进改革创新，不断塑造发展新动能新优势，充分激发全社会创造活力。	To properly handle the relationship between integrity and innovation, we must not only guard the origin and source, root and soul of Chinese-style modernization, unswervingly adhere to the Chinese characteristics, essential requirements and major principles of Chinese-style modernization, and ensure the correct direction of Chinese-style modernization, but also put innovation in a prominent position in the overall development of the country, conform to the development requirements of the times, focus on solving major theoretical and practical problems, actively identify and adapt to changes, vigorously promote reform and innovation, constantly shape new momentum and new advantages for development, and fully stimulate the creative vitality of the whole society.	no
效率是公平的重要基础，公平是效率的有力保证。	Efficiency is an important foundation for fairness, and fairness is a strong guarantee of efficiency.	no
我们推进中国式现代化，既要创造比资本主义更高的效率，又要更有效地维护社会公平，更好实现效率与公平相兼顾、相促进、相统一。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, we must not only create higher efficiency than capitalism, but also more effectively safeguard social fairness, and better realize the balance, promotion and unity of efficiency and fairness.	no
处理好效率与公平的关系，不断实现发展为了人民、发展依靠人民、发展成果由人民共享，让现代化建设成果更多更公平惠及全体人民。	We should properly handle the relationship between efficiency and fairness, continuously realize that development is for the people, development depends on the people, and the fruits of development are shared by the people, so that the fruits of modernization will benefit all the people more and more fairly.	no
推进中国式现代化，需要处理好活力与秩序的关系，让社会既充满活力又安定有序。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, it is necessary to properly handle the relationship between vitality and order, so that society is both dynamic and stable and orderly.	no
要统筹好发展和安全两件大事，贯彻总体国家安全观，健全国家安全体系，增强维护国家安全能力，坚定维护国家政权安全、制度安全、意识形态安全和重点领域安全。	It is necessary to make overall plans for the two major affairs of development and security, implement the overall concept of national security, improve the national security system, enhance the ability to maintain national security, and firmly safeguard the security of state power, system, ideology and key areas.	no
既在发展中更多考虑安全因素，通过发展提升国家安全实力，运用发展成果来夯实国家安全的基础，又善于营造有利于经济社会发展的安全环境，不断激发发展活力，实现高质量发展和高水平安全的良性互动。	It not only gives more consideration to security factors in development, enhances national security strength through development, and uses development achievements to consolidate the foundation of national security, but also is good at creating a security environment conducive to economic and social development, constantly stimulating development vitality, and achieving a benign interaction between high-quality development and high-level security.	no
推进中国式现代化，既要坚持走自己的路，又要拓展世界眼光，坚持对外开放，不断拓展中国式现代化的广度和深度。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, we must not only adhere to our own path, but also expand the world's vision, adhere to opening up to the outside world, and constantly expand the breadth and depth of Chinese-style modernization.	no
要坚持独立自主、自立自强，坚持把国家和民族发展放在自己力量的基点上，坚持把我国发展进步的命运牢牢掌握在自己手中。	We must persist in independence, self-reliance and self-improvement, persist in placing the development of the country and the nation on the basis of our own strength, and persist in firmly grasping the destiny of China's development and progress in our own hands.	no
要不断扩大高水平对外开放，深度参与全球产业分工和合作，用好国内国际两种资源，拓展中国式现代化的发展空间，在互利共赢中共享发展机遇、共创美好未来。	It is necessary to continuously expand high-level opening up, deeply participate in the global industrial division of labor and cooperation, make good use of domestic and international resources, expand the development space of Chinese-style modernization, and share development opportunities and create a better future in mutual benefit and win-win results.	no
循道而行，方能致远。	Only by following the path can we go far.	no
让我们在以习近平同志为核心的党中央坚强领导下、在习近平新时代中国特色社会主义思想科学指引下，把握规律、笃行不怠，充分发挥积极性、主动性、创造性，正确处理好一系列重大关系，在全面建设社会主义现代化国家新征程上奋发有为，不断开辟中国式现代化新境界。	Under the strong leadership of the Party Central Committee with Comrade Xi Jinping at the core and under the scientific guidance of Xi Jinping Thought on Socialism with Chinese Characteristics for a New Era, let us grasp the law, act resolutely, give full play to our enthusiasm, initiative and creativity, correctly handle a series of major relationships, work the new journey of building a modern socialist country in an all-round way, and constantly open up a new realm of Chinese-style modernization.	no
（德国之声中文网）拜登政府本周五（2月10日）将6个与疑似参与间谍气球计划的中国实体列入黑名单。	The Biden administration blacklisted six Chinese entities suspected of being involved in Chinese the spy balloon program this Friday (February 10).	yes
美国商务部表示，这5家中国公司及1家研究机构帮助中国军队现代化，尤其是航空航天项目，包括飞艇和飞机。	The Commerce Department said the five Chinese companies and one research institute helped modernize China's military, especially aerospace programs, including airships and aircraft.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司很难获得美国的技术出口。	Blacklisted companies have difficulty accessing U.S. technology exports.	yes
名单被称为“实体名单”（entity list），入列的公司除非获得美国商务部的特别出口许可证，否则将无法向美国供应商购买技术或商品。	The list is called an "entity list," and companies on the list will not be able to buy technology or goods from U.S. suppliers unless they have a special export license from the U.S. Department of Commerce.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司是：北京南江空天科技股份有限公司、中国电子科技集团第四十八研究所、东莞凌空遥感科技有限公司、鹰门航空科技集团有限公司、广州天海翔航空科技有限公司和山西鹰门航空科技集团有限公司。	The blacklisted companies are: Beijing Nanjiang Aerospace Technology Co., Ltd., the 48th Research Institute of China Electronics Technology Group, Dongguan Lingkong Remote Sensing Technology Co., Ltd., Yingmen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd., Guangzhou Tianhaixiang Aviation Technology Co., Ltd. and Shanxi Yingmen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd.	yes
在此之前，白宫表示考虑做出更广泛措施，“揭露和处理”中国威胁美国国家安全的更大规模监控活动。	That comes after the White House said it was considering broader measures to "expose and handle" China's larger surveillance activities that threaten U.S. national security.	yes
气球事件引发中美之间进一步紧张，美国国务卿布林肯取消了访问中国的行程。	The balloon incident sparked further tensions between China and the United States, with U.S. Secretary of State Antony Blinken canceling a trip to China.	yes
美国2月4日击落气球，中国政府向美国驻华使馆提出严正交涉，批评美国严重冲击和损害双方稳定中美关系的努力和进程。	When the United States shot down the balloon on February 4, the Chinese government lodged solemn representations with the US Embassy in China, criticizing the United States for seriously impacting and damaging the efforts and process of stabilizing Sino-US relations.	yes
从现有残骸证据及中国军方的采购平台资讯，美国政府得出结论，认为该气球的制造厂商“跟中国解放军有直接关系”，而且是中国军方批准的供应商。	From the available evidence of wreckage and information from the Chinese military's procurement platform, the U.S. government concluded that the manufacturer of the balloon was "directly related to the People's Liberation Army" and was an approved supplier by the Chinese military.	yes
中国外交部发言人毛宁在周五的新闻发布会上表示，关于一只中国无人民用飞艇因不可抗力误入美国领空的意外事件，中方已经多次说明情况、阐明立场。	Chinese Foreign Ministry spokesman Mao Ning said at a news conference on Friday that China has repeatedly explained the situation and stated its position on the accidental incident of a Chinese unmanned civilian airship mistakenly entering US airspace due to force majeure.	yes
根据外交部网站，她补充表示，美国国会的有关决议案纯属政治操弄和炒作。	According to the website of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, she added that the relevant resolutions of the US Congress are pure political manipulation and hype.	no
中方对此强烈不满、坚决反对。	China is strongly dissatisfied with and resolutely opposes this.	no
美国商务部负责出口执法的助理部长阿克塞尔罗德(Matthew Axelrod)表示： “今天的行动表明，我们查明并阻止中国使用间谍气球而做出的共同努力，这些气球侵犯了美国和40多个国家的领空。	Matthew Axelrod, Assistant Secretary for Export Enforcement at the U.S. Department of Commerce, said: "Today's action demonstrates our joint efforts to identify and deter China's use of spy balloons that violate the airspace of the United States and more than 40 countries.	no
”	”	no

（德国之声中文网）距离土耳其和叙利亚部分地区发生地震已经过去数日，找到幸存者的希望日渐渺茫，然而在周六获救的一家五口却令搜救人员感到无比欣慰。	Days after earthquakes struck parts of Turkey and Syria Chinese, there is little hope of finding survivors, but the rescue of a family of five rescued on Saturday is a source of great relief.	yes
据美联社报道，在加济安泰普省的重灾区努尔达伊镇，这个五口之家在废墟之下受困五天多之后，被成功营救。	In the hardest-hit town of Nurdayi in Gaziantep province, the family of five was successfully rescued after being trapped under rubble for more than five days, according to the Associated Press.	yes
搜救人员先是从一堆废墟中拉出了母亲和女儿，随后找到了父亲，但他坚持要求先救自己的儿子和另一个女儿。	Search and rescue crews first pulled the mother and daughter from a pile of rubble and then found the father, but he insisted that his son and another daughter be saved first.	yes
当他们全部获救之后，人群中响起了欢呼声。	When they were all rescued, cheers rang out from the crowd.	yes
在土耳其南部城市卡赫拉曼马拉什，在恶劣的严寒天气条件下，一个16岁的少年和一位70岁老妪也被成功营救。	In the southern Turkish city of Kahramanmaraş, a 16-year-old boy and a 70-year-old woman were also successfully rescued under harsh cold weather conditions.	yes
“今天是什么日子了？	"What day is it?	yes
”——这个被困废墟之下129小时的少年在被带回到地面上之后问营救自己的搜救员。	The teenager, who had been trapped under the rubble for 129 hours, asked the search and rescue workers who rescued him after being brought back to the ground.	yes

目前根据官方统计，周一的地震已经在土耳其造成超过2万人死亡，邻国叙利亚的死亡人数估计在3500人以上。	Monday's quake has killed more than 20,000 people in Turkey and is estimated at more than 3,500 in neighboring Syria, according to official statistics.	yes
尽管专家表示，人在被困废墟之后最多还能存活一周以上的时间，但是寻找到更多幸存者的希望已经变得愈加渺茫。	While experts say people can survive more than a week after being trapped in the rubble, the hope of finding more survivors has become increasingly slim.	no
救援人员仍然在借助热成像仪来探寻废墟之下的生命迹象。	Rescuers are still using thermal imagers to look for signs of life beneath the rubble.	no
与此同时，救援工作的重点开始转向帮助那些急需救助的幸存者。	At the same time, the focus of relief efforts has shifted to helping survivors in desperate need.	no
联合国官员：该地区“百年未遇”的灾难	UN official: A disaster "unseen in a century" in the region	no
主管人道主义事务的联合国副秘书长兼紧急救济协调员马丁·格里菲思（Martin Griffiths）在土耳其召开的记者会上表示，这次地震是该地区“百年以来最糟糕的一次灾难”。	Martin Griffiths, the UN Under-Secretary-General for Humanitarian Affairs and Emergency Relief Coordinator, told a news conference in Turkey that the quake was "the worst disaster in a century" in the region.	no
他还称赞土耳其在灾后的应对行动是“非同寻常”的。	He also praised Turkey's post-disaster response as "extraordinary."	no

60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
智利大地震（1960年）	Chile earthquake (1960)	no
当地时间1960年5月22日下午3点11分，智利瓦尔迪维亚发生人类史上观测记录到的规模最大的地震，地震矩规模为9.5。	At 3:11 p.m. local time on May 22, 1960, the largest earthquake recorded in human history occurred in Valdivia, Chile, with a seismic moment scale of 9.5.	no
短短十分钟内，瓦尔迪维亚整座城市变为废墟。	In just ten minutes, the entire city of Valdivia was in ruins.	no
地震之后引发的巨大海啸袭击到智利海岸线，掀起浪高高度是25米高的巨大海啸。	The huge tsunami that followed the earthquake hit the Chilean coastline, setting off a huge tsunami with a height of 25 meters.	no
海啸波及到遥远的日本、菲律宾。	The tsunami spread to distant Japan and the Philippines.	no
如此范围的灾难所造成的罹难人数以及经济损失无法精确得知。	The number of victims and economic losses caused by a disaster of this magnitude cannot be accurately known.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
阿拉斯加大地震（1964年）	Alaska Earthquake (1964)	no
1964年3月27日是一个星期五，也是是耶稣受难日。	March 27, 1964 was a Friday, which was also Good Friday.	no
这一天美国阿拉斯加发生北美洲历史上最大的地震，矩震级达到9.2。	On this day, the largest earthquake in North American history struck Alaska, USA, with a moment magnitude of 9.2.	no
直到2006年，阿拉斯加大地震仍然是有纪录以来世界第三大地震。	Until 2006, the Alaska earthquake remained the third largest earthquake on record.	no
地震发生时，太平洋板块和北美洲板块之间的一个断层在威廉王子湾接近学院峡湾的地方断裂。	At the time of the earthquake, a fault between the Pacific Plate and the North American Plate broke near the College Fjord in Prince William Sound.	no
在大部分的地区这场地震持续了3分钟到5分钟。	In most areas, the earthquake lasted between 3 and 5 minutes.	no
海床位移引发了巨大的海啸，高度为67米。	The displacement of the seabed caused a huge tsunami with a height of 67 meters.	no
由于当天是假日，所以学校和许多企业都关闭了。	Since it was a holiday, schools and many businesses were closed.	no
这场大地震最后导致了139人罹难。	The earthquake killed 139 people.	no
其中9人直接死于地震，其他130人死于地震引发的海啸。	Nine of them died directly from the earthquake and the other 130 died as a result of the tsunami triggered by the earthquake.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
唐山大地震（1976年）	Tangshan Earthquake (1976)	no
1976年7月28日，中国河北省唐山市和丰南县在16小时内发生两次7级以上强烈地震。	On July 28, 1976, two strong earthquakes of magnitude 7 or higher struck Tangshan City and Fengnan County in Hebei Province, China.	no
震源距地面23千米。	The epicenter is 23 kilometers above the ground.	no
唐山市全市交通、通讯、供水、供电中断，顷刻间被夷为平地。	Transportation, communications, water supply and power supply in Tangshan City were interrupted and razed to the ground in an instant.	no
140公里外的首都北京也有强烈震感。	The earthquake was also felt in the capital Beijing, 140 kilometers away.	no
据官方统计，包括北京、天津在内的所有受灾地区，地震造成242769人死亡，164851人重伤。	According to official statistics, the earthquake killed 242769 people and seriously injured 164851 in all affected areas, including Beijing and Tianjin.	no
唐山大地震成为中国有记录至今第二多人死亡的地震，仅次于1556年嘉靖大地震。	The Tangshan earthquake became the second most fatal earthquake recorded in China, after the 1556 Jiajing earthquake.	no
但是有海外科学家估计，这场地震可能造成至少65万人死亡。	But some overseas scientists estimate that the quake may have killed at least 650,000 people.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
印度洋大地震（2004年）	Indian Ocean Earthquake (2004)	no
2004年12月26日，印尼苏门答腊岛亚齐省西岸160公里处发生地震，震源深度30公里，矩震级9.1到9.3。	On December 26, 2004, an earthquake occurred 160 km west of Aceh Province on the Indonesian island of Sumatra, with a focal depth of 30 km and a moment magnitude of 9.1 to 9.3.	no
地震引发了浪高高度达15到30米的巨大海啸。	The earthquake triggered a huge tsunami with waves of 15 to 30 meters high.	no
太平洋沿岸总共14个国家被波及，其中受灾严重最严重的地区包括印尼亚齐省、泰国镐立和普吉岛渡假区、斯里兰卡和印度泰米尔邦。	A total of 14 countries along the Pacific coast were affected, with the hardest-hit areas including the Indonesian province of Aceh, the resorts of Ho Li and Phuket in Thailand, Sri Lanka and the Indian state of Tamil Pradesh.	no
当时正值圣诞节的旅游旺季，受灾地区聚集了大量的旅客和本地居民，导致许多在沙滩上享受假期的旅客和在海边工作的当地人被海啸卷到海底，使这次地震不少人成为失踪者。	It was the peak tourist season for Christmas, and a large number of tourists and local residents gathered in the affected area, resulting in many tourists enjoying holidays on the beach and locals working by the sea being swept to the bottom of the sea by the tsunami, making many people missing from the earthquake.	no
据估计，罹难人数和失踪人数至少有30万人。	It is estimated that at least 300,000 people have been killed and missing.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
汶川大地震（2008年）	Wenchuan Earthquake (2008)	no
2008年5月12日，中国四川省汶川地区发生大地震。	On May 12, 2008, a major earthquake struck the Wenchuan area of Sichuan Province, China.	no
根据中国地震局的数据，此次地震的面波震级达8.2级、矩震级达8.3级，破坏地区超过10万平方公里。	According to the China Earthquake Administration, the earthquake had an area wave magnitude of 8.2 and a moment magnitude of 8.3, and the damage area exceeded 100,000 square kilometers.	no
截至2008年9月25日，地震共计造成69227人遇难，17923人失踪，374643人不同程度受伤，1993.03万人失去住所，受灾总人口达4625.6万人。	As of September 25, 2008, the earthquake had killed a total of 69,227 people, 17,923 people were missing, 374643 were injured to varying degrees, and 19,930,300 people lost their homes, bringing the total number of people affected to 46,256,000.	no
是中华人民共和国成立以来破坏力最大的地震，也是唐山大地震后伤亡最惨重的一次。	It is the most destructive earthquake since the founding of the People's Republic of China, and it is also the heaviest casualty after the Tangshan earthquake.	no
2009年3月，中国国务院宣布将每年的5月12日定为防灾减灾日，加强对民众的教育和对防灾减灾工作的关注。	In March 2009, the State Council of China announced that May 12 of each year would be designated as Disaster Prevention and Mitigation Day to strengthen education and attention to disaster prevention and mitigation.	no
之后中国多地政府和中小学在每年这一天举行防震演习。	Since then, governments and primary and secondary schools in many places in China have held earthquake drills on this day every year.	no
中小学也开始重视普及“防震减灾”教育。	Primary and secondary schools have also begun to pay attention to universal education on "earthquake prevention and disaster reduction".	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
海地地震（2010年）	Haiti earthquake (2010)	no
2010年1月12日，加勒比海岛国海地发生里氏7.0级的地震。	On January 12, 2010, an earthquake measuring 7.0 on the Richter scale struck the Caribbean island nation of Haiti.	no
震中位于海地首都太子港以西南方25公里，震源距离地表13千米左右。	The epicenter was located 25 kilometers southwest of Port-au-Prince, Haiti's capital, and the epicenter was about 13 kilometers above the surface.	no
国际红十字会估计，受到地震影响的人口大约为300万。	The International Committee of the Red Cross estimates that approximately 3 million people were affected by the earthquake.	no
海地政府公布的确认死亡人数超过20万。	The Haitian government has announced more than 200,000 confirmed deaths.	no
海地国内的一些地区，多达90%的房屋在地震中被摧毁。	In some parts of Haiti, as many as 90 per cent of houses were destroyed in the earthquake.	no
虽然国际社会提供了大量援助和支持，但是这个人口过剩腐败横行的贫困国家从未从这场灾难中恢复过来。	Despite substantial assistance and support from the international community, this impoverished and corrupt country has never recovered from the disaster.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
日本东北大地震（2011年）	Great Tohoku Earthquake (2011)	no
2011年3月11日日本东北地方外海发生矩震级为9.0的大型逆冲区地震。	On March 11, 2011, a large thrust zone earthquake with a moment magnitude of 9.0 struck off the coast of Tohoku, Japan.	no
震中位于在宫城县首府仙台市以东的太平洋海域，震源深度测得数据为24千米，并且引发最大爬高40.1米的巨大海啸。	The epicenter was located in the Pacific Ocean east of Sendai City, the capital of Miyagi Prefecture, and the depth of the epicenter was measured to be 24 kilometers, and a huge tsunami with a maximum climb of 40.1 meters was triggered.	no
这场地震是日本有观测纪录到以来第一个震级超过9的地震。	The earthquake was the first earthquake recorded in Japan to exceed magnitude 9.	no
约有2.2万人在灾害丧生，大约40万座建筑被完全摧毁或倒塌。	Some 22,000 people were killed in the disaster and about 400,000 buildings were completely destroyed or collapsed.	no
福岛第一核电站受地震海啸影响发生泄漏事故。	The Fukushima Daiichi Nuclear Power Plant was affected by an earthquake and tsunami and a leakage accident.	no
这次事故在国际核事件分级表（INES）中被分类为最严重的7级。	The accident was classified as the most severe level 7 in the International Nuclear Event Classification Scale (INES).	no
福岛核事故导致在全世界都测量到微量辐射性物质，包括碘-131、铯-137（半衰期为30年）在内。	The Fukushima nuclear accident resulted in the worldwide measurement of trace amounts of radioactive substances, including iodine-131 and cesium-137 (half-life of 30 years).	no
大量放射性同位素因此核事故释入太平洋。	A large number of radioisotopes were released into the Pacific Ocean as a result of the nuclear accident.	no
根据联合国的统计，在土叙两国灾区，目前至少有87万人急需食物。	According to United Nations statistics, at least 870,000 people in the disaster areas of Turkey and Syria are in urgent need of food.	no
仅仅在叙利亚，就有多达530万人因为地震而失去家园。	In Syria alone, as many as 5.3 million people have lost their homes to the earthquake.	no
世界粮食计划署（WFP）呼吁拨款7700万美元，为土耳其和叙利亚因为地震而流离失所的灾民提供食物。	The World Food Programme (WFP) has appealed for $77 million to feed people displaced by the earthquake in Turkey and Syria.	no
目前灾区气温低至零下，很多灾民没有住所。	At present, the temperature in the affected area is as low as freezing, and many of the affected people have no shelter.	no
土耳其政府分发了大量的热餐、帐篷和毯子，但是这些物资仍然难以送达很多急需帮助的人。	The Turkish government has distributed large quantities of hot meals, tents and blankets, but these supplies are still struggling to reach many people in need.	no
而在深陷内战泥潭长达12年之久的叙利亚，地震则使民众的苦难处境雪上加霜。	And in Syria, which has been mired in civil war for 12 years, the earthquake has exacerbated the misery of the population.	no
在地震发生后的四天内，世界粮食计划署已经向土耳其和叙利亚的11.5万人提供了食物救济。	Within four days of the quake, WFP had provided food relief to 115,000 people in Turkey and Syria.	no
世界卫生组织（WHO）则送去了72吨用于外伤处理和紧急手术的医药物资。	The World Health Organization (WHO) sent 72 tonnes of medical supplies for trauma management and emergency surgery.	no

NEWS GOV-MO: 警情通告：司警局呼吁市民提防假冒电讯公司诈骗短讯	NEWS GOV-MO: Police Notice: The Police Force urges members of the public to watch out for fraudulent text messages from counterfeit telecommunications companies	yes
近日司警局接获多宗电信诈骗案，不法分子假冒本澳电讯公司向事主发送附有网站连结的诈骗短信，以积分到期须尽快换领奖赏为饵，诱骗事主登入虚假网站进行兑换。	Recently, the Judicial Police Bureau has received a number of telecommunications fraud cases in which criminals impersonate local telecommunications companies to send fraudulent text messages with website links to the subjects, using the bait that the points must be redeemed as soon as possible when they expire, tricking the victims into logging on to the fake websites for redemption.	yes
事主按指示输入信用卡资料及验证码，随即收到金融机构通知信用卡出现不明消费记录，怀疑信用卡资料经上述网站被盗取。	The subject entered the credit card information and verification code as instructed, and immediately received a notification from the financial institution that the credit card had an unknown consumption record, and suspected that the credit card information had been stolen through the above website.	yes
经查，证实相关电讯公司并无发出上述短讯。	After investigation, it was confirmed that the relevant telecommunications company did not send the above SMS.	yes
司警局呼吁市民，如接获类似手机短讯须提高警惕，切勿登入短讯所载网站连结或提供任何个人资料；若被要求提供信用卡资料、帐户交易密码、交易验证码，更要加倍谨慎，防止信用卡被盗刷。	The Police Force urges members of the public to be vigilant when receiving similar SMS messages and not to log in to the websites contained in the SMS or provide any personal data; If you are required to provide credit card information, account transaction password, transaction verification code, you should be extra cautious to prevent credit card theft.	yes
防骗提示：	Anti-scam tips:	yes
1. 多关注网络安全资讯，提高个人防范意识；	1. Pay more attention to network security information and improve personal awareness of prevention;	yes
2. 切勿随便登入来历不明的网站并在网站内登记个人及信用卡资料，以防遭人盗用；	2. Do not log in to websites from unknown sources and register personal and credit card information on the websites to prevent theft;	yes
3. 警惕假冒网站及钓鱼网站，时刻留意网站网址是否与官方网站完全相符；	3. Be wary of fake websites and phishing websites, and always pay attention to whether the website URL is completely consistent with the official website;	yes
4. 为手机、移动装置或电脑安装防毒软件，并定期更新；	4. Install anti-virus software for mobile phones, mobile devices or computers, and update them regularly;	yes
5. 怀疑遇到诈骗或其他犯罪时，应立即致电司警局防诈骗查询热线8800 7777或报案热线993求助。	5. If you suspect that you have encountered fraud or other crimes, you should immediately call the Fraud Prevention Enquiry Hotline of the Police Force at 8800 7777 or the Reporting Hotline 993 for assistance.	no

新华社北京2月10日电 中共中央总书记、国家主席、中央军委主席习近平2月9日给第19批援助中非共和国的中国医疗队队员回信，向他们以及广大援外医疗队员致以问候并提出殷切期望。	Beijing, 10 Feb (Xinhua) -- On 9 February, Xi Jinping, general secretary of the CPC Central Committee, state president, and chairman of the Central Military Commission, wrote back to the 19th batch of members of the Chinese medical team assisting the Central African Republic, extending greetings and ardent expectations to them and the vast number of medical team members assisting foreign countries.	yes

援外医疗是我国援外工作的重要内容。	Foreign aid medical care is an important part of China's foreign aid work.	yes
1963年，我国向阿尔及利亚派出第一支援外医疗队。	In 1963, we sent the First Support Foreign Medical Corps to Algeria.	yes

重阳问答︱如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	Chongyang Q&A—How to view the US non-farm payrolls data in January exceeded expectations and future trends - Economic Observer Network - Professional financial news website	yes
Q：请问重阳投资，如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势？	Q: How do you view the US non-farm payrolls data in January exceeding expectations and future trends?	yes
A：2月3日美国劳工部公布2023年1月非农就业数据，新增非农就业51.7万人，大幅高于市场预期的18.9万人；失业率降至3.4%，为近50年以来的最低位；时薪同比增速4.4%，环比增速0.3%，略有放缓。	A: On February 3, the US Department of Labor released non-farm payrolls data for January 2023, adding 517,000 non-farm payrolls, significantly higher than market expectations of 189,000; the unemployment rate fell to 3.4%, the lowest level in nearly 50 years; Hourly earnings grew 4.4% year-over-year and 0.3% month-on-month, slowing slightly.	yes
从总量上来看，本次数据存在很多一次性和技术性因素的扰动，比如罢工返岗的教职工、调查统计口径的修正、季调因子的更新，后续可能将有所修正（参考2022年1月新增非农由50.4万人下修至36.4万人），非农就业或不像数据体现的那样强劲。	From the total point of view, there are many one-time and technical factors in this data, such as the return of teachers and staff from strike, the revision of the survey statistical caliber, and the update of the seasonal adjustment factor, which may be revised in the future (referring to the new non-farm payrolls revised down from 504,000 to 364,000 in January 2022), and non-farm payrolls may not be as strong as the data reflects.	yes
从结构上来看，高科技企业裁员影响仍在，但占比较低；高接触性服务业如休闲酒店、教育保健等新增就业大幅回升，数据显示服务业劳动力缺口仍存。	From a structural point of view, the impact of layoffs in high-tech enterprises is still there, but the proportion is relatively low; New jobs in high-touch service industries such as leisure and hospitality, education and health care have rebounded sharply, and the data shows that the labor gap in the service industry still exists.	yes
结合同样大超预期的服务业PMI、岗位空缺和劳动力缺口数据的回升和消费信贷数据的强势，我们判断经过极端天气和节假日后美国服务业迎来了快速修复。	Combined with the recovery in the same better-than-expected services PMI, job openings and labor gap data and strong consumer credit data, we judge that the US services sector has ushered in a rapid recovery after extreme weather and holidays.	yes
我们认为，在不经过衰退的情况下美国就业市场的供需紧张难以改善。	In our view, the tight supply and demand in the U.S. job market is unlikely to improve without a recession.	yes
目前美国劳动力市场尚有500余万的供给缺口，而劳动参与率上行缓慢，尤其是25-54岁劳动参与率已经接近疫情前高点。	At present, there is still a supply gap of more than 5 million yuan in the US labor market, and the labor participation rate is slowly rising, especially the labor force participation rate for 25-54 years old is close to the pre-epidemic high.	yes
除此之外，由于美国居民超额储蓄和消费信贷的强势，消费需求的强劲将促使紧缩政策对就业市场的影响进一步滞后。	In addition, due to the strength of excess savings and consumer credit in the United States, strong consumer demand will further delay the impact of tightening on the job market.	yes
美国就业市场供需持续紧张将是2023年美国经济的底色。	The continued tight supply and demand in the US job market will be the background color of the US economy in 2023.	yes
叠加目前临近加息结束，通胀预期不断反复，我们对薪资增速的持续下降并不乐观。	Coupled with the fact that the end of the interest rate hike is nearing and inflation expectations are constantly repeating, we are not optimistic about the continued decline in wage growth.	no
本次数据公布前，美国股债汇市场对于美联储加息路径的预期过于乐观。	Before the release of this data, the US stock and bond exchange market was too optimistic about the Fed's interest rate hike path.	no
随着通胀数据的持续改善，美联储在缩短加息步伐的同时还不断维系着市场通胀预期脆弱的平衡，但市场对于美联储偏向鹰派的表述视而不见，不仅预期提前停止加息，还预期年末两次降息。	As inflation data continues to improve, the Fed has shortened the pace of interest rate hikes while maintaining a fragile balance of market inflation expectations, but the market has turned a blind eye to the Fed's hawkish statements, not only expecting to stop raising interest rates early, but also expecting two rate cuts at the end of the year.	no
在劳动力市场供需紧张，紧缩政策影响不明的情况下，我们认为美联储年末对于加息的指引是相对合理的，市场极端预期的调整和交易的拥挤或将对市场产生一定伤害。	In the context of tight supply and demand in the labor market and unclear impact of tightening policies, we believe that the Fed's guidance for interest rate hikes at the end of the year is relatively reasonable, and the adjustment of extreme market expectations and crowded trading may cause some harm to the market.	no
尽管如此，薪资增速的顽固难改当前通胀快速下降的趋势，随着M2数据同比转负以及各个CPI分项领先指标的逐渐转好，自10月份以来美国CPI数据已经转向快速下降阶段，薪资增速的顽固仅会对以后的通胀数据形成托底，当前的市场预期难以证伪，在下一期通胀数据公布后市场或进入新一轮博弈。	Nevertheless, the stubbornness of wage growth is difficult to change the current trend of rapid decline in inflation, with the M2 data turning negative year-on-year and the gradual improvement of various CPI sub-leading indicators, since October the US CPI data has turned to a rapid decline stage, the stubbornness of wage growth will only form a foundation for future inflation data, the current market expectations are difficult to falsify, and the market may enter a new round of game after the next inflation data is released.	no
杉杉创始人郑永刚因突发心脏疾病过世 曾带领中国服装第一股转型 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	Shanshan founder Zheng Yonggang passed away due to sudden heart disease and led the transformation of China's first garment stock - Economic Observation Network - Professional financial news website	yes
经济观察网 记者 郑淯心 2月11日，认证主体为杉杉控股有限公司（以下简称“杉杉控股 ” ） 的微信公众号发布讣告，杉杉企业创始人、杉杉控股董事局主席郑永刚因突发心脏疾病救治无效，于2023年2月10日去世，享年65岁。	Economic Observation Network Reporter Zheng Huixin On February 11, the WeChat public account of Shanshan Holdings Co., Ltd. (hereinafter referred to as "Shanshan Holdings") released an obituary that Zheng Yonggang, founder of Shanshan Enterprises and chairman of the board of directors of Shanshan Holdings, died on February 10, 2023 at the age of 65 due to ineffective treatment of sudden heart disease.	yes
上世纪80年代，郑永刚担任国营棉纺厂的厂长，随着调任，1989年郑永刚成为杉杉股份的前身宁波云港服装总厂的厂长。	In the 80s of last century, Zheng Yonggang served as the director of the state-owned cotton spinning factory, and with the transfer, in 1989 Zheng Yonggang became the director of Ningbo Yungang Garment General Factory, the predecessor of Shanshan Co., Ltd.	yes
2022年12月，在第二十届中国企业领袖年会暨第二十二届中国企业未来之星年会上，郑永刚在演讲中称，在上世纪90年代的中国西服市场，杉杉品牌的市占率曾高达37 % 。	In December 2022, at the 20th Annual Meeting of Chinese Business Leaders and the 22nd Annual Meeting of Future Stars of Chinese Enterprises, Zheng Yonggang said in his speech that in the Chinese suit market in the 90s of last century, the market share of the Shanshan brand was as high as 37%.	yes
1996年杉杉股份（600884.SH）上市，成为中国服装业第一家上市公司。	In 1996, Shanshan shares (600884. SH) went public, becoming the first listed company in China's garment industry.	yes
就在服装业务如日中天时，杉杉集团却开始转型，因为郑永刚意识到 ， “ 一旦市场放开，中国品牌自然会形成一个梯队式品牌市场，杉杉西服想一直独领风骚，长期成为国人的国服的可能性不大 ” 。	Just when the clothing business was in full swing, Shanshan Group began to transform, because Zheng Yonggang realized that "once the market is opened, Chinese brands will naturally form an echelon brand market, and Shanshan Suit wants to always lead the way, and it is unlikely that it will become the national uniform of Chinese people for a long time".	yes
1999年，杉杉开始研究企业转型，郑永刚回忆当年 ， “ 我们来到上海，寻求到底转型做什么，专门找了很多专家学者，连续不断地开一些诸葛亮会、务虚研讨会。	In 1999, Shanshan began to study enterprise transformation, and Zheng Yonggang recalled, "We came to Shanghai, looking for what the transformation did, and specially found many experts and scholars, and continuously held some Zhuge Liang meetings and retreat seminars.	yes
最后，我们设定了两个大的战略方向。	In the end, we set two broad strategic directions.	yes
第一个方向是新能源新材料，另外一个是大健康有未来 ” 。	The first direction is new energy and new materials, and the other is that great health has a future."	yes
战略方向确定后，杉杉开始寻找合作，那时候鞍山热能院为鞍钢配套的炭素研究所在做国家863课题，科研经费不够，于是杉杉和鞍山热能院碳素研究所签署合作协议，共同推动国家863课题“中间相炭微球”项目产业化，从事负极材料的研发、生产和销售，在国内实现负极材料的商用推广。	After the strategic direction was determined, Shanshan began to look for cooperation, at that time, Anshan Thermal Energy Institute for Angang supporting the carbon research institute was doing the national 863 project, scientific research funds were not enough, so Shanshan and Anshan Thermal Energy Institute Carbon Research Institute signed a cooperation agreement to jointly promote the industrialization of the national 863 project "mesophase carbon microspheres" project, engaged in the research and development, production and sales of anode materials, and realize the commercial promotion of anode materials in China.	yes
2001年，杉杉股份实现中间相炭微球的规模化生产，开始国产化替代，取代日本成为国内中间相炭微球主要供应商。	In 2001, Shanshan Co., Ltd. realized the large-scale production of mesophase carbon microspheres and began to replace it locally, replacing Japan as the main supplier of mesophase carbon microspheres in China.	no
这是中国第一家锂离子电池负极材料生产企业，实现了锂离子电池负极材料国产化。	This is the first lithium-ion battery anode material manufacturer in China, and has realized the localization of lithium-ion battery anode materials.	no
随着锂电池的应用迅速普及，杉杉股份的锂电池业务开始逐步发展，2007年锂电材料业务被写入了杉杉股份的主营业务，服装业务营收占比逐年减少，直至2013年，杉杉股份的锂电材料业务收入全面超过服装业务。	With the rapid popularization of the application of lithium batteries, the lithium battery business of Shanshan Co., Ltd. began to develop gradually, in 2007, the lithium battery material business was written into the main business of Shanshan Co., Ltd., and the proportion of clothing business revenue decreased year by year, until 2013, Shanshan Co., Ltd.'s lithium battery material business income fully exceeded the clothing business.	no
2021年2月，杉杉股份成功并购LG化学偏光片业务，进军LCD偏光片市场，并成立偏光片企业杉金光电，该领域技术含量比较高，杉杉的主要的竞争对手都是世界500强，如韩国三星、日本的住友化学、日东电工。	In February 2021, Shanshan Co., Ltd. successfully acquired LG Chem's polarizer business, entered the LCD polarizer market, and established a polarizer enterprise Shanjin Optoelectronics, which has a relatively high technical content in this field, and Shanshan's main competitors are the world's top 500, such as South Korea's Samsung, Japan's Sumitomo Chemical, and Nitto Denko.	no
郑永刚曾分享过投后管理的心得 ， “ 中国的民营企业收购国际上的一些高科技企业，成功概率比较低，为什么那些收购会失败？	Zheng Yonggang once shared his experience in post-investment management, "China's private enterprises acquire some international high-tech enterprises, the probability of success is relatively low, why do those acquisitions fail?	no
因为大家都会去考虑，我花了那么多钱，我得去派人管对吧，这是通常会做的一个行为 ” ， 然而郑永刚则不同，杉杉收购成功的那一天，郑永刚就到杉金光电当众宣布，杉杉作为杉金的大股东，决定实施一企两制，除了郑永刚担任董事长，杉杉企业的人不派到杉金，采取授权经营的方式，原有的分配制度、企业文化、各项管理等模式不变。	Because everyone will think about it, I spent so much money, I have to send someone to manage it, right, this is an act that is usually done", but Zheng Yonggang is different, the day of the successful acquisition of Shanshan Zheng, Zheng Yonggang went to Shanjin Optoelectronics to announce in public that Shanshan as the major shareholder of Shanjin, decided to implement one enterprise and two systems, except for Zheng Yonggang as the chairman, the people of Shanshan enterprise are not sent to Shanjin, and the original distribution system, corporate culture, various management and other models remain unchanged.	no

“基金E账户”来了：证监会授权开发 投资者名下所有基金实现归集和查询 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	"Fund E Account" is coming: China Securities Regulatory Commission authorizes the development of all funds under the investor's name to achieve aggregation and inquiry - Economic Observation Network - Professional financial news website	yes
经济观察网 记者 陈姗 基金购买渠道繁杂导致账户信息归集不易？	Economic Observation Network Reporter Chen Shan Fund purchase channels are complicated, resulting in account information aggregation is not easy?	yes

2月10日，证监会公告称，“基金E账户”APP在各手机应用商店上架并开展公开试运行。	On February 10, the China Securities Regulatory Commission announced that the "Fund E Account" APP was launched on various mobile app stores and carried out public trial operation.	yes
据介绍，“基金E账户”为个人投资者提供公募基金账户及份额信息的“一站式”查询服务，旨在解决广大中小投资者遗忘账户、查询繁琐等行业服务痛点。	According to reports, the "Fund E Account" provides individual investors with a "one-stop" inquiry service for public fund account and share information, aiming to solve the pain points of industry services such as forgetting accounts and cumbersome inquiries for the majority of small and medium-sized investors.	yes
据Wind数据显示，截至2022年底，国内共有公募基金管理人156家，管理基金规模约26万亿元；公募基金份额登记机构167家，公募基金销售机构411家。	According to Wind data, by the end of 2022, there were 156 public fund managers in China, with a fund size of about 26 trillion yuan; There are 167 public fund share registration institutions and 411 public fund sales institutions.	yes
各份额登记机构账户体系相互独立，缺乏行业统一的查询渠道。	The account systems of each share registration institution are independent of each other, and there is no unified inquiry channel for the industry.	yes
有行业人士表示，2021年末我国基金投资者超过7.2亿人，也就是说，全国有一半人都投资了基金产品。	Some industry insiders said that at the end of 2021, there were more than 720 million fund investors in China, that is, half of the country's people invested in fund products.	yes
此前，投资者需要通过不同销售机构查询购买情况，而通过“基金E账户”可以查询所有销售渠道购买的情况，持有基金情况一目了然。	Previously, investors needed to inquire about purchases through different sales institutions, but through the "Fund E Account" they could inquire about the purchase of all sales channels, and the holding of funds was clear at a glance.	yes
“基金E账户”APP是什么？	What is the "Fund E Account" app?	no
据相关文件介绍，“基金E账户”APP 是中国结算经中国证监会批准开发建设的公募基金行业门户手机应用，可为投资者提供全市场公募基金产品场外份额持有情况的一站式查询。	According to relevant documents, the "Fund E Account" APP is a mobile application for the public fund industry portal developed and constructed by China Clearing with the approval of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, which can provide investors with one-stop inquiry of the over-the-counter share holdings of public fund products in the whole market.	no
投资者可以通过“基金E账户”方便、快捷地掌握自己通过全市场各销售渠道购买的各基金管理人旗下公募基金产品场外份额的持有情况，全面提升查询效率。	Through the "Fund E Account", investors can conveniently and quickly grasp the holdings of the over-the-counter shares of each fund manager's public fund products purchased through various sales channels in the whole market, and comprehensively improve the efficiency of inquiry.	no
具体来说，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”查询到的信息包括：在全市场各公募基金管理人处开立的基金账户信息、在公募基金销售机构处开立的交易账户信息以及持有的包括公开募集证券投资基金以及证券公司设立管理的投资者人数不受200人限制的集合资产管理计划等产品的场外份额持有情况。	Specifically, the information that investors can inquire through the "Fund E Account" includes: fund account information opened with public fund managers in the whole market, trading account information opened with public fund sales institutions, and over-the-counter share holdings of products including publicly offered securities investment funds and collective asset management plans with a number of investors established and managed by securities companies that are not limited to 200.	no
上海证券基金评价研究中心业务负责人刘亦千向经济观察网记者表示，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”App一站式获知其所有的场外公募基金持有情况，帮助其找回“被遗忘的资产”，更重要的是为客户实现了综合基金投资情况的全账户信息归集，帮助客户更及时、准确、完整的掌握自身投资情况，从而更好地优化自身的基金组合配置，更好地规划自身的财务安排。	Liu Yiqian, head of business of Shanghai Securities Fund Evaluation and Research Center, told the Economic Observation Network reporter that investors can get all their over-the-counter public fund holdings through the "Fund E Account" App in one stop, help them recover "forgotten assets", and more importantly, realize the collection of comprehensive fund investment information for customers, help customers grasp their own investment situation more timely, accurately and completely, so as to better optimize their fund portfolio allocation and better plan their financial arrangements.	no

上海一家中大型公募基金客服人员向经济观察网记者提供了一个6位数的邀请码，并告诉记者，“APP试运行阶段，中国结算提供给每个基金管理人一定数量的邀请码，投资者电话过来获取，我们都会提供。	The customer service staff of a medium and large public fund in Shanghai provided a 6-digit invitation code to the Economic Observation Network reporter, and told the reporter, "During the trial operation of the APP, China Clearing provided each fund manager with a certain number of invitation codes, and investors will provide them by phone."	no

东德共产党的继任者在该党在一份声明中报告，“昨晚，汉斯·莫德罗 (Hans Modrow) 离开了我们，享年 95 岁。	The successor of the Communist Party of East Germany reported in a statement that "last night, Hans Modrow left us at the age of 95.	yes
因此，我们的党失去了一位重要领导人。	As a result, our party lost an important leader.	yes
”	”	yes
1989 年 11 月 13 日，在将东柏林和西柏林分开 28 年的柏林墙打开四天后，莫德罗曾表示他将帮助把东德变成一个民主国家。	On November 13, 1989, four days after the opening of the Berlin Wall, which separated East and West Berlin for 28 years, Modero had said he would help turn East Germany into a democracy.	yes
当时，由于东德各地的抗议者要求民主和自由，共产党领导人被迫下台。	At that time, Communist leaders were forced to step down as protesters across East Germany demanded democracy and freedom.	yes
戈尔巴乔夫 (Mikhail Gorbachev) 在苏联上台后曾要求在苏联主导的东欧也进行变革。	After coming to power in the Soviet Union, Mikhail Gorbachev called for changes in Soviet-dominated Eastern Europe as well.	yes
1990 年 3 月，莫德罗宣布德意志民主共和国 (GDR) 的第一次也是唯一一次自由选举。	In March 1990, Modro announced the first and only free elections for the German Democratic Republic (GDR).	yes
选举结果导致他不再担任总理。	As a result of the election, he was no longer prime minister.	yes
尽管莫德罗进行了改革，但反对者指责他试图推迟 1990 年 10 月发生的政治变革和统一。	Despite Modero's reforms, opponents accused him of trying to delay the political changes and unification that took place in October 1990.	yes
他还因试图重塑而不是废除秘密警察而受到批评。	He has also been criticized for trying to reinvent, rather than abolish, the secret police.	no
1993 年，莫德罗在 1989 年 5 月的市政选举中被判选举舞弊罪名成立，但并未入狱。	In 1993, Modero was convicted of electoral fraud in the May 1989 municipal elections but was not jailed.	no
有称这些指控是出于政治动机。	The allegations were said to be politically motivated.	no
1990 年至 1994 年，莫德罗继续在德国议会任职，并于 1999 年至 2004 年担任欧洲议会议员。	From 1990 to 1994, Modro continued to serve in the German Parliament and was a member of the European Parliament from 1999 to 2004.	no
莫德罗将自己视为一名改革者，并希望从内部改变共产党。	Modro sees himself as a reformer and wants to change the Communist Party from within.	no
1999 年，他告诉路透社，他不希望旧东德回归，但表示应该承认东德的成就。	In 1999, he told Reuters he did not want the old East Germany to return, but said East Germany's achievements should be acknowledged.	no
莫德罗于 1928 年出生在当时的德国小镇 Jasenitz（现为波兰的 Jasienica），并接受过机械师培训。	Modero was born in 1928 in the then German town of Jasenitz (now Jasienica, Poland) and trained as a mechanic.	no
第二次世界大战期间，他担任青年消防队排长，并在冲突快结束时成为纳粹民兵组织 Volkssturm 的一员，该组织征召 16 至 60 岁的男子参加最后的战争挣扎。	During World War II, he served as a platoon leader for the youth fire brigade and, towards the end of the conflict, became part of the Nazi militia Volkssturm, which recruited men between the ages of 16 and 60 to fight in the final struggles of war.	no
17 岁时，莫德罗被苏联军队俘虏，作为战俘被带到苏联，在那里他参加了反法西斯课程，并成为一名坚定的共产党员。	At the age of 17, Modeso was captured by the Soviet army and taken to the USSR as a prisoner of war, where he took anti-fascist courses and became a staunch communist.	no
1949 年，即东德成立的那一年，他回国后找到了一份机械师的工作，并继续学习社会科学和经济学，并获得了博士学位。	In 1949, the year East Germany was founded, he returned home and found a job as a mechanic and continued to study social sciences and economics, where he received a doctorate.	no
莫德罗是自由德国青年运动的一名工作人员，几乎所有东德年轻人都加入了该运动，并在 1973 年至 1989 年期间通过执政的社会统一党 (SED) 晋升为德累斯顿地区党的主席。	Modero was a staff member of the Free German Youth Movement, which almost all young people in East Germany joined and rose to chair of the Dresden Regional Party between 1973 and 1989 through the ruling Socialist Unity Party (SED).	no
他还在东德任职议会超过 30 年。	He also served as the parliament of East Germany for more than 30 years.	no

阿拉斯加上空被击落的 “物体”究竟是什么？	What exactly is the downed "object" over Alaska?	yes
扑朔迷离，猜测纷纷	Confused, speculative	yes
美国军方周五（2月10日）下午再次动用美国最先进的隐身喷气战机F-22击落了一个在美国阿拉斯加上空飞行的尚未确定身份的物体。	On Friday (February 10) afternoon, the U.S. military again used the U.S. most advanced stealth jet F-22 to shoot down an unidentified object flying over Alaska, USA.	yes
击落的地点距离阿拉斯加海岸十英里。	The shot down site was ten miles off the coast of Alaska.	yes
这是美军在不到一周的时间里第二次击落空中飞行物体。	This is the second time in less than a week that the U.S. military has shot down an airborne object.	yes
上周六，来自中国的一个间谍气球在美国领空上漂移数日后在美国南卡罗莱纳州沿岸附近上空被击毁。	On Saturday, a spy balloon from China drifted over U.S. airspace for days before being destroyed off the coast of South Carolina.	yes
五角大楼说，第二个被击落的物体于周四晚上首次进入美国领空，在阿拉斯加东北部上空移动时被美国军方跟踪，飞行高度为1.2万米（4万英尺），其大小与一辆小型汽车差不多，与先前被击落的那个中国间谍气球相比要小很多。	The Pentagon said the second downed object, which first entered U.S. airspace Thursday night and was tracked by the U.S. military as it moved over northeast Alaska, flying at an altitude of 12,000 meters (40,000 feet) about the size of a small car and much smaller than the Chinese spy balloon that had been shot down earlier.	yes
五角大楼还认为，目前没有迹象显示，这个物体是可操纵的。	The Pentagon also believes that there is currently no indication that the object is manipulable.	yes
白宫国家安全委员会战略沟通协调员约翰·科比周五表示，虽然这个在高空飞行的物体的具体样子尚不清楚，但它“对民航飞机的安全构成了合理的威胁”。	John Bryant, the White House National Security Council's strategic communications coordinator, said Friday that while the exact appearance of the high-altitude object is unclear, it "poses a reasonable threat to the safety of civilian aircraft."	yes
科比表示，这个物体与美国境内发现的那个间谍气球不同，它上面没有悬挂“有效载荷”。	Bryant said the object, unlike the spy balloon found in the United States, did not have a "payload" hanging from it.	yes
科比说，“我们把它称为一个‘物体’是我们目前能够作出的最好的描述”。	"We call it an 'object' the best we can describe it right now," Bryant said.	no
拜登总统在下令击落这个物体之前听取了五角大楼的建议，他作出这个决定的时候“非常谨慎”，科比补充说。	President Biden, who listened to the Pentagon's advice before ordering the shooting down of the object, was "very cautious" in making the decision, Bryant added.	no
美国官方对这个物体的描述大致可以归纳为：大小相当于一辆小汽车，没有操纵杆，没有悬挂装置，飞行高度为一万米左右。	The official description of this object in the United States can be roughly summarized as: the size of a small car, no joystick, no suspension device, and the flight altitude is about 10,000 meters.	no
但这些信息还无法回答基本问题，比如这个物体究竟是什么东西，它属于哪个国家，它在执行什么任务。	But this information doesn't yet answer basic questions, such as what the object is, which country it belongs to, and what mission it is performing.	no
目前网上许多的分析和猜测认为，这可能又是一只中国气球。	At present, many analysis and speculation on the Internet believe that this may be another Chinese balloon.	no
它可能与入侵美国领空的那只间谍气球和在拉美上空飘动的那只中国气球一样都来自中国，它们在不同地点执行某种任务。	It may have originated from China like the spy balloon that invaded U.S. airspace and the Chinese balloon that fluttered over Latin America, performing some kind of mission in different locations.	no
也有人把阿拉斯加的这个“物体”与“不明飞行物”（UFO）联系在一起。	Others associate this "object" in Alaska with a "UFO."	no
美国新闻周刊的报道引用美国前众议员彼得·梅杰（Peter Meijer）周五在推特上发出的推文说，“真希望这个‘不明飞行物’也是一个间谍气球，而不是一个合法的UFO”。	The U.S. Newsweek report quoted former U.S. Representative Peter Meijer as tweeting on Friday as saying, "I wish this UFO was also a spy balloon and not a legitimate UFO."	no

决定一个人工作满意度的第一要素不是薪水高低，而是在工作中是否得到了足够重视和赏识。	The first factor that determines a person's job satisfaction is not the level of salary, but whether they are valued and appreciated enough at work.	yes
根据马斯洛需求层次理论，在人的基本生存需要得到满足后，最迫切的就是心理需要的满足——希望被理解、被肯定、被赏识。	According to Maslow's hierarchy of needs, after the basic survival needs of people have been satisfied, the most urgent thing is the satisfaction of psychological needs—the desire to be understood, affirmed, and appreciated.	yes
